Important News

Chiang Kai-shek's New Year Aspirations 60

Two Most Important Matters for the Twentieth Year of the Republic

Respect Education and Encourage Agriculture

Today is the New Year's Day of the twentieth year of the Republic. As the new year begins, all compatriots nationwide must be thinking about making vigorous efforts to improve themselves daily. I, Chiang Kai-shek, wish to present two extremely important matters to my compatriots and hope that we can all work together. What are these two matters? They are emphasizing education and revitalizing agriculture. Since the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee, the guidelines for local administration for this year have been established. The focus of national effort should be on post-military affairs and the suppression of the Communists and bandits. However, the passive reorganization of politics must be supplemented by active measures, and the work of treating symptoms must rely on the cultivation of the root cause. I have seen that the Three People's Principles of governance require maximizing land use, human talent, resource utilization, and unhindered flow of goods. These goals are aligned with the virtues of good governance from ancient China, such as respecting education, encouraging learning, valuing talent, training agriculture, facilitating commerce, and benefiting labor. Therefore, nation-building must prioritize the people's livelihood, and the most urgent needs of the people's livelihood are education and sustenance. In China today, I dare say that respecting education and encouraging agriculture are especially important. China's industry and commerce have already achieved some initial progress in response to the natural trends of economic development. It only requires removing restrictions and eliminating excessive interference to allow vitality to flourish and prosperity to grow daily. The government has spared no sacrifice to abolish likin (internal customs tax) and is implementing it as scheduled. It is also determined to realize the reorganization of finance and the promotion of investment in a gradual manner. As for education and agriculture, they are not only preconditions for the development of all industries but also the foundation for stabilizing national order. It is essential that all compatriots understand this and act accordingly, and then we can unite our efforts to achieve success. I will now present these two matters to all compatriots. First, let me speak of education. In recent years, there has been some progress in all aspects of society in China, but education alone has not only failed to improve but has also declined daily. The literacy rate among the people is less than 20%. Social education is extremely lacking, let alone the education at all levels from universities to primary schools. Very few schools can be compared to those in civilized countries in terms of facilities, teachers, and teaching achievements. The breakdown of school discipline and the decline in educational effectiveness are unprecedented in ancient and modern times, both at home and abroad. Parents have never stopped sending their children to schools, but they do not ask about the significance of educating their children. They believe that their responsibility is complete once they have sent their children to school. Teachers have never stopped claiming to be educators, but they do not consider their responsibilities to the nation, the people, and the students. Most teachers treat their work as a means of earning a living and calculate their worth by the hour. Students have never stopped progressing through the grades, but they do not want to hear about the discipline they should observe as students. They do not care about the cultivation they should have in academics and skills. They do not consider their responsibilities to the nation, the people, and their own future. They only accumulate years of experience to prepare for future employment. There are certainly some sound and sincere individuals among them, but the majority are like this: the mediocre are content with idleness, the rebellious are accustomed to disobedience, and the dissolute indulge in leisure. Education in other countries aims to cultivate healthy citizens, but most schools in our country only cultivate vagrants, rioters, and even deficient people lacking in both mind and skill. It is already regrettable that people in remote areas lack access to education. Those who have the opportunity to receive education are either misguided or untrained. Is this not a hidden concern for society and the nation? It is already sad that students do not respect their teachers, but it is even more tragic that teachers do not strive to be respected and instead demean themselves into irresponsible knowledge vendors. Given the lack of universal education in our country and the current state of education, how can we prevent the children of our country from being buried and sacrificed under the lack of education, becoming either victims who are easily tempted to become reactionaries or useless individuals lacking any skills? The loss of stability in social order and the loss of foundation for all construction are all due to this. If this continues without any attempt to remedy the situation, it not only goes against the Three People's Principles of maximizing human talent, but the disaster of national subjugation and racial extinction will be imminent. I hope that people in society will see this danger clearly and regard educating children as a serious responsibility, making the support of education and the cultivation of talent the most sacred duty to the nation, assisting the government, supervising the schools, reviving the defunct, strengthening the weak, and correcting the wrong. The whole nation should unite and regard this as the most important task of this year. This is one. Secondly, let me speak of agriculture. The decline of agriculture in our country is not a recent phenomenon. The oppression of international economic aggression, the devastation of warlord tyranny, the rampant activities of the Communist bandits, and the ignorance of farmers have all contributed to the decline of agricultural production and the impoverishment of rural areas. This has led to a decrease in raw material exports and an increase in reliance on foreign food imports. Those who advocate reform, seeing the trends of the world economy and the progress of agriculture, believe that emphasizing industry and commerce is necessary to establish a country in the modern world. Others believe that it is necessary to fundamentally reform agricultural production methods, replacing small-scale manual production with large-scale mechanized farming. However, they do not realize that the major reasons for the decline of agriculture are half due to poor methods and techniques, and half due to the farmers being affected by poor politics, leading to displacement, hardship, and inability to focus on farming. In the past thirty years, due to the influence of international aggression and poor politics, the fact that the domestic social foundation has not completely collapsed is largely due to the fact that over 80% of farmers are still working diligently and enduring hardship. Therefore, the fundamental plan is to strive to improve production methods, and at the same time, if we can alleviate the suffering of farmers, stabilize rural order, and actively encourage the increase of agricultural production, even if we use existing techniques and methods to engage in production, it will be enough to increase national wealth and enrich the people. Looking at the agricultural harvests in most parts of the country last year, they were generally abundant, and within the areas of abundant harvests, bandit activity decreased sharply, refugees gradually gathered, and grain prices plummeted. Although farmers did not gain significant benefits, the nation and society have benefited immensely. This alone is enough to demonstrate the importance of agriculture. What should be noted is that we cannot rely on favorable weather conditions, and we must not fail to exhaust human effort. Even with last year's abundant harvest, it is still difficult for rural areas to recover from their exhaustion. If there is even a slight natural disaster this year, then after the recent cessation of warfare and the incomplete suppression of bandits, the suffering will easily lead to displacement. I believe that the majority of the people in China are farmers, and the poverty and chaos in recent years have been largely due to the fact that the central figures of society have flocked to the cities, leaving the countryside increasingly empty and the fields unattended. There is no greater danger to the nation than this. Therefore, the urgent task today is to have all compatriots recognize the importance of encouraging agriculture. Parents should instruct their children, and villagers should encourage their neighbors to unite and strive to increase agricultural production. As for suppressing bandits, establishing Baojia (household registration system), promoting agricultural cooperatives, and circulating agricultural funds, all means of stabilizing and enriching the countryside should be vigorously pursued by the government and society. As for managing water conservancy and developing transportation, the government has already made these the top priority and will do its utmost to promote them. In short, everyone in the country should understand China's national conditions and make promoting agriculture the most important task of this year. This is another. Sun Yat-sen said that the purpose of revolution is to save the country. How can the country be saved? It must start with saving the people. The effect of saving the people relies on self-reliance. Education is a long-term plan, and agriculture is entrusted with the lives of the majority. I hope that all compatriots in the country will unite and focus on the fundamental aspects of these two matters. I, Chiang Kai-shek, though lacking in ability, have high expectations.

19th Route Army Captures Wan'an and Taihe 61

Wang Jin-yu Advances to Suppress the Kong and Li Bandits in Xiu and Tonggu

Nanchang dispatch: The 60th and 61st Divisions of the 19th Route Army are responsible for suppressing bandits on the west bank of the Gan River. After recapturing Lianhua and Yongxin on the border of Jiangxi and Hunan provinces, the 19th Route Army split into two routes, heading towards Wan'an on the east bank of the Gan River and Taihe on the west bank, hoping to cross the Gan River from Wan'an and encircle the bandits in Xingguo, and to coordinate with the Ma brigade of the 12th Division. According to a telegram from Gu'an, the Qu brigade of the 60th Division recaptured Wan'an on the 22nd and can connect with the Ma brigade. The Zhang brigade of the 61st Division occupied Taihe on the 20th, forming a unified front with the Luo, Zhang, and other divisions in Ji'an and Jishui. The bandits' fake 22nd Army have all been routed, opening up transportation on the upper reaches of the Gan River. Shipping from Ji'an to Ganzhou can be restored. The headquarters of the 19th Route Army moved from Yongxin to Wan'an on the 23rd. Wan'an is connected to Xingguo in the east, Ganzhou in the south, and borders Nankang and Suichuan on the right. It is a necessary route from the province to Ganzhou. It has recently been occupied by bandits, cutting off transportation between Ji'an and Ganzhou. Hundreds of merchant ships were detained here, unable to go up or down, and economic activity was cut off. Now it is seeing the light of day again, and travel should be unimpeded in the future. As for the Pingxiang area, it was originally an important town on the border of Jiangxi and Hunan. It is heard that Wang Jin-yu will set up a Bandit Suppression Command on the border of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi in Pingxiang, to clear the Communist bandits in Pingxiang, Wanzai, Tonggu, Xiushui, and Pingjiang, Liuyang in Hunan, and Tongcheng, Chongyang, and Tongshan in Hubei. It is understood that the bandit leaders here are Kong Hechong and Li Shixing. After capturing Xiushui, they advanced towards Wuning and Tonggu, and a small force invaded Fengxin, acting very rampantly. Hao Mengling of the 54th Division has already dispatched a brigade from Fengxin to Xiushui, and sent a part from Jiujiang to reinforce Wuning, hoping to cooperate with Wang Jin-yu's troops, advancing north along the border of Jiangxi and Hunan towards the border of Hubei, and annihilating the Li and Kong bandits. (December 29th)

Large Number of Communists Executed in Wuhan 62

Fifteen Men and Women Including Su Limin

Hankou dispatch: The Wuhan Garrison Command, because Wuhan is located in a strategic location and many Communist bandits are hiding there, specially dispatched dedicated personnel to investigate and arrest them day and night. In recent months, it has cracked down on about a dozen secret Communist organizations and arrested over a hundred important Communist members. Recently, it cracked down on another Communist organization. The leaders Su Limin and others were responsible as members of the Communist Yangtze River Committee, presiding over the joint uprisings in the five provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Sichuan, and Henan. After strict interrogation by the Garrison Command, all the uprising plans were revealed, and on the 27th, Su Limin and 14 others were brought out and executed by firing squad. The charges are recorded as follows: 1) According to the Investigation Department of this Command, nine important Communist criminals, Su Limin, Yuan Bingzhang, Yuan Shuren, Zhang Xiaoqing, Yi Shuya, Li Guanghui, Yang Zhisiao, Hu Yunqing, and Deng Congxin, were arrested, and many reactionary declarations and plan drafts were seized. They were all sent to the Command for interrogation. After opening the court and conducting detailed interrogation, Su Limin confessed that he was formerly the secretary of the Fujian Communist Provincial Committee and was recently transferred by the Central Committee to serve as a member and secretary-general of the Yangtze River Bureau. He presided over many of the reactionary plans in the five provinces of Hubei, Hunan, Jiangxi, Sichuan, and Henan. Yuan Bingzhang confessed that he was formerly the secretary of the Hunan Communist Provincial Committee and was transferred this year to serve on the Sichuan Provincial Military Committee. He came to Wuhan recently to attend the preparatory meeting for organizing the joint uprising of the five provinces and discuss the implementation methods. Yuan Shuren confessed that he was formerly a cadre of the Organization Department of the Communist Central Committee and served concurrently in the Military Work of the Military and Political Action Committee. Recently, due to the destruction of the Wuhan Communist organization, he was ordered to come to Wuhan to plan to restore the organization and rigorously implement armed uprisings. Zhang Xiaoqing and Yi Shuya jointly confessed that they were ordered by the Yangtze River Bureau to become husband and wife and establish a reception organization specifically to accommodate party members participating in the uprising. Li Guanghui and Yang Zhiqing jointly confessed that they both served as technical secretaries of the Yangtze River Bureau and were ordered to establish a printing organization, jointly responsible for mimeographing. Hu Yunqing confessed that he was responsible for the transportation work of the Yangtze River Bureau and was ordered to cooperate with Deng Congxin and others of the Hanchuan County Committee to establish a transportation organization. The above confessions are not denied. Recently, the Communist organizations in Wuhan have been thoroughly investigated and cracked down on by this Command. The local areas have been cleaned up, and the clearing can be seen day by day. However, the criminals still dared to establish organizations, recruit bandit leaders, plan to restore organizations, and vainly attempt to expand the uprising. They were truly incorrigible and reckless. They should all be sentenced to death according to the law to show a clear warning. In addition to signing and submitting the criminals, verifying their identities, and binding them to the execution ground to be executed by firing squad, a public announcement is hereby issued to make it known to all. 2) According to the Third Regiment of the Central Gendarmerie, a Communist criminal Xu Yunping, who was found to be carrying reactionary publications, was handed over to this Command. After opening the court and repeatedly studying the case, and after self-confessed persons testified in court, it was confirmed that the criminal had joined the Communist Party and served in the Wuchang District Committee and in various important positions in the Hankou Municipal Committee after attending a Communist meeting in Shanghai. In this way, the criminal is an important member of the Communist Party and performs important duties. His crime is heinous and cannot be tolerated by the law. He should be sentenced to death in accordance with Article 2, Paragraph 2 of the Law on Punishing Counter-Revolutionaries to show a clear warning. In addition to signing and submitting the criminal, verifying his identity, and binding him to the execution ground to be executed by firing squad, a public announcement is hereby issued to make it known to all. 3) According to the Investigation Department of this Command, two Communist bandits, Yu Fengqi and Fu Hanzhang, were arrested and handed over to this Command. After repeated investigation, the bandit Yu Fengqi confessed that he joined the Communist Party, mobilized peasants, established rural groups, and was responsible as the group leader, preparing for armed uprisings. Fu Hanzhang confessed that he joined the Communist Party, served in the Jiang'an District organization work, mobilized peasants to establish rural groups, gathered fugitive vagrants, prepared for armed uprisings to respond to the Red Army, and received 15 yuan in living expenses from the Communist Party. The confessions are straightforward and undeniable. In this way, they joined the Communist Party, performed important duties, and intended to carry out armed uprisings. The circumstances are serious and cannot be tolerated by the law. They should be sentenced to death in accordance with Article 2, Paragraph 2 of the Law on Punishing Counter-Revolutionaries. In addition to verifying their identities and binding them to the execution ground to be executed by firing squad, a public announcement is hereby issued to make it known to all. 4) According to the Investigation Department of this Command, three Communist criminals, Xiong Wei, Lu Jia, and Liu Gengqi, were arrested and submitted to this Command for interrogation according to the law. After opening the court for interrogation and having the confessed persons testify in court, it was confirmed that Tai Wei joined the Communist Party, served as the secretary of the Soldiers' Committee, and received funds. He established a military transport organization in Qianjia Street, Nanhu, to receive Communist soldiers. Lu Jia previously served in the Ye He bandit army, participated in the Haifeng and Lufeng uprisings in Guangdong, and carried out burning and killing indiscriminately. This time, he secretly came to Wuhan to take charge of military transport work in Wuchang. Liu Gengqi previously served as a private in the Nanjing Gendarmerie and planned an uprising. He was once wanted but not captured. Recently, he secretly came to Wuhan from Shanghai and cooperated with Xiong Wei and Lu Jia, intending to incite the National Army and carry out an uprising. All of the above facts are confirmed. The crimes are serious and cannot be excused. In addition to signing and submitting the criminals, verifying their identities, and binding them to the execution ground to be executed by firing squad, a public announcement is hereby issued to make it known to all. Important News Two

Wang Jin-yu Takes Office 63

as the Commissioner of Bandit Suppression and Rural Pacification in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi Provinces

Hankou Dispatch: During his recent tour from Nanjing to Hubei, Generalissimo Chiang has formulated concrete plans for the bandits and Communists in the three provinces, dividing the areas for pacification and setting a deadline for complete suppression. He has also appointed Wang Jin-yu, the commander of the Ninth Army, as the Commissioner of Bandit Suppression and Rural Pacification in the border areas of the three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, and all commanders of the first, second, third, fourth, fifth, and sixth districts will be under his command for specific responsibilities. After receiving the order, Wang Jin-yu, considering the urgent nature of military affairs, took office first in Hankou on the 26th. The Commissioner's Office was originally located in Pingxiang, but Wang Jin-yu, after considering the situation, decided to temporarily set it up in Hankou and has telegraphed Generalissimo Chiang on the 27th to request instructions. Once approved, he will organize and establish it immediately. The Wuhan Headquarters, to ensure thoroughness in suppressing bandits in the three provinces simultaneously and to prevent them from fleeing and rising up, has formulated joint defense measures for the three provinces and appointed Liu Jianxu, the commander of the Tenth Army, as the director of the joint defense zone of the three provinces to oversee everything. The counties planned to be included in the joint defense zone are Changsha, Pingjiang, Liuyang, Liling, Xiangxiang, and Baling in Hunan; Chongyang and Tongshan in Hubei; and Pingxiang, Wanzai, Xiushui, and Tonggu in Jiangxi, totaling twelve counties. The joint defense can be implemented within about a week. As for the bandit situation in the three provinces, apart from Hunan and Jiangxi provinces, where they have been actively suppressed and suffered huge losses, and no longer have the ability to fight, great progress has also been made in Hubei province in recent days. For example, Songzi, Shishou, and Gong'an counties have been successively recaptured by Chen Cheng and Li Jue's troops, and Tongcheng, which was recently captured by the bandits, has also been recaptured by Zhou Xiwu's brigade of Tao Guang's unit. The remnants of the Huang'an bandits have also been wiped out by Su Zhichu's unit. The commanders of the Tao and Xiao divisions both telegraphed the Wuhan Headquarters on the 26th to report their victory. (December 27th)

The Circumstances of Li Yong'an's Troops Surrendering Their Weapons 64

The 52nd Division Was Ordered to Execute the Task

Li and His Troops Were Disarmed and Awaited Orders in Xu

Xu Prefecture Dispatch: The 52nd Division, under Han Deqin, was ordered to resolve the matter of Li Yong'an's independent brigade of the 8th Army, stationed in Xiao County. From the morning of December 26th to noon on the 28th, the entire situation was resolved. The circumstances are recorded as follows:

Disarmament Outside the City: On the morning of the 26th, Zhang Zhong, commander of the 154th Brigade of the Han Division, led the first regiment from Sanbao on the Jinpu Railway to the south of Xiao County. The third regiment marched from Yanglou on the Longhai Railway to the west of Xiao County. At dawn, the third regiment of Li's troops, under Lu Chongmin, was stationed in Meicun Wanzhuang, southwest of the city. The second regiment, partially led by Li Zijiang, was stationed in Duanyuan, northwest of the city, and Huatan Temple, south of the city. All were asleep. The first regiment of the Han Division launched a sudden attack on Meicun Wanzhuang, immediately resolving the entire Lu regiment and capturing Commander Lu Chongmin. The third regiment of the Han Division simultaneously resolved the Li troops in Duanyuan and Huatan Temple. Only a few troops escaped into the city amidst the chaos. As soon as it dawned, the escaped troops closed the city gates and defended the city. Brigade Commander Zhang counted over two hundred guns and captured four to five hundred men outside the city. He immediately ordered his troops to surround the city and fired machine guns at Li's troops on the city walls. He also had the division's orders delivered through the cracks in the city gate, ordering them to surrender immediately.

Surrounding the City and Negotiations: The people of Xiao County, suddenly hearing gunfire in their sleep, were unaware of the situation. County Magistrate Gan Gongyu sent personnel to inquire with Li's brigade headquarters. Lu Senxuan, Li's chief of staff, informed them that the 52nd Division had surrounded Xiao, fearing it was for disarmament. Upon receiving this news, Gan immediately ordered the police brigade to concentrate for self-defense at the county government, the police station, and the two watchtowers on the north and south streets. At the same time, he ordered Yang Jingzhi, head of the Public Security Bureau, to gather police for protection. The Xiao police force had three hundred guns, led by Captain Ma Ziliang. Fortunately, they were all in the city. They also constructed fortifications in front of the county government, stacking stones into walls, to prepare for any action by Li's brigade. They then inquired with the 52nd Division headquarters via long-distance telephone and reported the situation for instructions. At noon, Han Deqin personally led troops to Xiao, spoke with Wang via telephone, and delivered official documents over the city walls, ordering Wang to lead the local self-defense forces to seize the East Gate and meet the advancing army. Wang sent Wang Yuzhang, head of the General Affairs Section, and Shi Zhanru, representative of the Finance and Property Department, out of the city on ropes, raised a white flag on the city wall, and requested a temporary cessation of the attack. At the same time, he sent representatives Li Gongda, Zhang Penglai, Yin Gengye, Niu Lin, etc., to Li's brigade headquarters to negotiate with Li Yong'an, asking him to surrender his weapons and guaranteeing no further problems. After several twists and turns, by noon on the 27th, Li sent his mother, his four wives, and the families of his officers out as hostages. The Han Division then withdrew and retreated. Han ordered Li's troops to leave the city and surrender their weapons in Duanyuan. Li's troops hesitated. That evening, Han increased the encirclement again. Wang then sent people to spread news in all directions to shake the morale of Li's troops. Soldiers of Li's troops secretly surrendered to the county government, and Wang kept them in separate rooms. Li's confidants checked the troops in the city and found that their numbers were gradually decreasing. Realizing that he had no power and no way to escape, he convened a meeting of his officers that evening and decided to comply with the order to surrender their weapons. Thus, at dawn on the 28th, they surrendered their weapons to the county government. Those who had disarmed went to Duanyuan, west of the city, to assemble. Before disarming, Li sent Wang an orchid score, requesting an oath of brotherhood. Wang replied that there was no danger. Li then stayed at the county government. At this time, the Han Division had entered the city and sent troops to monitor Li. His senior officers and confidants were also monitored at the county government. The four gates were then opened. The county government collected about three hundred guns of various sizes, and Li's brigade headquarters also surrendered some guns. Han entered the city in the forenoon with county government representatives Wang Yuzhang and Wang Zhanru. The city's markets had been closed for three days and gradually resumed business.

Local Aftermath: During the siege and attack, the Han Division used machine guns and mortars to suppress Li's troops. Over ten shells landed in the city, one in the Public Security Bureau's office, one in the Normal School, two in the Education Bureau, two in front of the County Party Department, and two at the West Gate, killing three people: Hu Xuezhi, Hu the Lame, and a Jia surname youtiao seller. Over ten houses were destroyed. A shell landed outside the West Gate, igniting a fire and burning three or four thatched houses. Other buildings, such as the Farmers' Education Center, suffered slight damage, but there was no major harm. County Magistrate Wang Gongyu is currently working with local circles to handle the aftermath. Han Deqin yesterday appointed Battalion Commander He Dake as the city defense commander, responsible for maintaining治安. Brigade Commander Zhang Zhongfu returned to Xu yesterday with Han and went to Xiao this morning to oversee the aftermath and bring the detained Li brigade officers to Xu for telegraphic presentation to Chairman Chiang and Commander-in-Chief Liu for review and processing. Xiao City is still under strict guard, but the locality has returned to normal.

Li's Conversation: The reporter had a brief conversation with Li at the Xiao County Government. Li appeared to be about thirty years old, dressed in plain clothes, a long robe, a leather cap, and a cloak. He was smoking opium and seemed quite straightforward. He said that his unit was placed under the command of the 2nd Army Corps Commander Liu Zhi last winter and commissioned as the temporarily compiled 2nd Brigade Commander. This summer, when the Western Route War started, it was changed to the command of the 8th Army as an independent brigade. After the war, it was stationed in Bozhou. It was only moved to Xiao County on the 16th of this month. He did not know that he was transferred here for disarmament. He had always obeyed orders, so he had no intention of resisting this time, and so on. Li's Chief of Staff, Lu Senxuan, was also present at the time. His right ear was missing. At the moment, Li, Lu, and his regimental commanders Li Zelin, Lu Chongmin, Secretary Tao Pinshan, Adjutant Zhu Zhizhong, Deputy Regimental Commander Yin Shanmin, Battalion Commander Li Lanqing, Li Keyong, followers Chen Yougong, Hu Kunyi, Jia Chengen, Li Kezhong, Li Kebin, Li Kexing, Yang Wentian, etc., were all escorted to Xu by car. According to investigation, Li's brigade had a total of three regiments and four special service companies. Li was the brigade commander and concurrently the commander of the second regiment. The first regiment commander was Li Zelin, and the second regiment commander was Lu Chongmin. The total strength was 3,300 men, but the actual number was less. Only over a thousand people have been captured, and a small number of scattered soldiers took the opportunity to escape west. (December 29th)

The Tragedy of Burning Narcotics in Jinan 65

Explosives Were Mixed into the Burning Narcotics

One Person Died on the Spot, More Than Ten Were Seriously Injured

Jinan Dispatch: This morning (29th) at 9:00 AM, the Jinan Municipal Government burned opium, smoking paraphernalia, heroin, and other narcotics in front of the city hall. The fire brigade first poured the narcotics into a pit, sprinkled them with several barrels of kerosene, and then ignited them. About ten minutes after ignition (around 10:00 AM), there was a sudden explosion. The sound of the explosion was heard throughout the city. At the time, government officials and spectators scattered and fled, and order was thrown into chaos. About twenty minutes later, personnel from the municipal government and the Public Security Bureau went forward to inspect the scene. Liu Xishan, a policeman from the fire brigade, was killed on the spot by the explosion. Others who were injured included Liu Zizhan, Secretary of the Provincial Government; Yang Shisheng, Chief of the General Affairs Section of the Municipal Government; Qian Zhuo, Director of the Document Section; Tu Zhizhang, clerk of the Business Section; Li Shutong, clerk; Ma Zedong, Director of the Administrative Section; Secretary Ni Dewei; and fire brigade policemen Lian Shouchang, Fei Fuchang, Chen Junsheng, Han Qinfang, and Wang Rongfu (severely injured). The seriously injured were immediately taken to Jinan Hospital for emergency treatment. The cause of the explosion was that there was an iron box in the narcotics. Prior inspection was not done before burning. It contained yellow-wrapped explosives, said to have been left behind by the retreating Jin army. Because its color was similar to the narcotics, it was included in the narcotics and burned together, resulting in this unexpected tragedy. It is reported that Ma Zedong, the Chief of the Administrative Section of the Municipal Government, was seriously injured and may be in critical condition. The killed policeman, Liu Xishan, was from Dong'e and lived in Jinan. He left behind an old mother and a young sister. His mother and sister are currently wailing and preparing the body for burial. The municipal government's relief measures are currently being discussed. (29th)

A Record of Visiting Ancient Relics in Tan City 66

Jinan Dispatch: The Ancient Site Research Association, jointly formed by the Academia Sinica and the Shandong Provincial Government, excavated the old Tan State city of Chengzhiya, Longshan Town, east of Jinan City, and obtained a large number of ancient relics. After stopping the excavation, for several weeks of sorting work, each ancient object was washed with water, and the broken ones were glued together. The ancient objects were specially displayed and an exhibition was opened, scheduled for January 1st and 2nd. The arrangements have now been completed. I visited the exhibition yesterday and recorded the general situation as follows:

Overview of the Exhibition Room: The address of the exhibition is the Engineering College of Qingdao University, in the office of the Ancient Site Research Association in the north house of the third courtyard (i.e., the physics laboratory of the former Industrial School). There are three rooms, and each ancient object is classified and displayed. Generally, the middle room contains various charts, the east room contains cultures before the Tan State, mostly stone tools and bone tools, and the west room contains Tan State culture and other ancient objects, such as pottery and bricks.

General Situation of Ancient Object Arrangement: In the east room, there are stone axes, stone knives, and stone hammers on the south table, some thick and blunt, some thin and sharp, which are thought to have gradually evolved. There is a piece of white jade, as big as an inkstone, round on the upper side and square on the bottom side. There is a small hole, which may be used for wearing. It has been determined to be a thing from before the Han Dynasty. Among the coins, there is half of a Qi knife, with raised lines on it, which is quite fine. There are quite a few bone-made utensils, such as needles, awls, and hairpins, all of which are placed in glass boxes. There is a cow scapula, which is an ancient divination tool, with dense traces of fire burning. The round holes are spotted and impermeable. The ancients looked at the shape of the cracked lines to predict good and bad luck. There are also many bones that have not been manufactured. There are horn utensils on the east table, mostly deer antlers made into sharp shapes, used as weapons. The clam shells have very fine serrations, and there are also several large clam shells that can be a foot in diameter, as well as snail shells, the small ends of which have been removed, which proves that ancient

Page 16

people also liked this thing very much. There are black pottery on the north table, all of which have been pieced together from fragments with glue. One or two objects can be as much as 80% intact. There are even more thin fragments, all placed in boxes. From here, one enters the middle room. On the wall is an imaginary map of Tan City, made square, 450 meters long and wide. There are also seven pieces of Tan City, with the rammed earth marks clearly visible. There are also stove ashes, made of chopped wheat straw mixed with soil, just like today's method. The traces of wheat straw are still identifiable. From here, one enters the west room. On the west table are white pottery, a three-legged Jia missing one foot. The gray pottery is mostly Dou and Li. There is a Ding that is quite complete. On the south table, there is a gray pottery, like a bell shape upside down on the ground, hollow, with two circular sections. The lower section has a slightly larger factory mouth, and the upper section is a small bowl, covered on the lower section, small and extremely unique. Its name is not known. On the south table are ancient relics from the vicinity of Linzi, the capital of Qi, and the Qi King's tomb, bricks and tiles, bones, etc., and there are also ancient relics from the ancient Pinglu City, three miles east of Tan City, also mostly bricks and tiles, etc. There are even objects from Tang Dynasty tombs in Tan City, two magnetic bottles, shaped like piggy banks, several green silks, very shiny, filled with rice, which has rotted, and a hat, the inside being cloth and the outside resembling leather, and a leather belt, with a copper buckle, which is very similar to today's. There are also various arrowheads, copper, stone, clam, bone, and pottery. On the middle table are pottery with colorful art, with patterns on them, and characters like "ten mountains and rivers," etc., which have not yet been identified as what characters they are. There are many mud balls, like the iron balls used for sports today, which were found five meters in the soil. It is not known what they are.

The Most Precious Ancient Relics: Among the ancient relics of Tan City culture and pre-Tan culture, there are those from 3,000 years ago, which have made significant contributions to archeology. Among them, pottery and arrowheads were discovered for the first time. Furthermore, the black pottery is of a strange and ancient style, black and shiny, which archeologists have never seen before, and is also one of the important right-hand tools after the excavation of the Yin Ruins. Furthermore, the clam saw is extremely sharp and has never been seen before. The cow scapula divination tool is certainly a Shang Dynasty item, contemporaneous with turtle shell divination, all of which are extremely important discoveries. (

December 27th).

Gong Debai Requests the Abolition of Private Tolls in Western Hunan 67

Gong Debai's letter to Zhang Fuyun, Director of the Customs Administration, stated: Your department is keen to abolish likin, eliminating this decades-long abusive policy. All Chinese people cannot but rejoice. I am originally from Western Hunan and know that the corner of Western Hunan has long been a land beyond the pale. Not only is it beyond the reach of central authority, but even the Hunan provincial government has no means to reach it. In the past, there were two warlords in Western Hunan, Chen Quzhen and Chen Hanzhang, each levying taxes and extorting money in their defense areas. The people were under the weight of oppression and had long dared to be angry but dared not speak out. Even if they did, the government would not hear it. Last year, Chen Hanzhang was assassinated and his troops disintegrated, but his defense area had been occupied by others. Currently, the only warlord who continues to do evil is Chen Quzhen. Chen's fixed defense area includes Yuanling, Luxi, Qiancheng, Fenghuang, Yongshui, Mayang, Guzhang, Yongshun, Baojing, Longshan, Sangzhi, and other counties, spanning the You River and Wu River basins (both tributaries of the Yuan River). Except for Yuanling County, which has more convenient transportation and the provincial government's eyes and ears are more attentive, Chen Quzhen does not dare to arbitrarily set up customs to levy taxes. However, from Yuanling to the north, tracing the You River from Luxi and westward, tracing the Wu River, there are customs every few miles or dozens of miles. The tax levied at each customs is heavier than the national tax. For goods with a likin of one yuan, the tax levied by Chen Quzhen's privately established customs is also around one yuan when transported to the destination. Such shocking things are not only unknown to the central government, but the Hunan provincial government is also deaf to them. Even if they hear about it, they cannot do anything about it. Now that likin has been completely abolished nationwide, these privately established customs should also be abolished. However, the effect of your department's circular can only extend to areas within the reach of the Hunan provincial government's authority, and it is extremely difficult to have any effect on these special areas under the iron heel of warlords. I urge you to convey this to Minister Song and send a strict telegram to the Hunan provincial government, ordering Chen Quzhen to abolish all these privately established customs. If he dares to disobey, please punish him severely. Only in this way can the corner of Western Hunan have the hope of seeing the light of day again. I respectfully offer nine bows on behalf of the people of Western Hunan to thank you.

Suzhou 68

Yu Tang Township Opens a Horticultural Specialty School: Minister Niu of the Ministry of Personnel, in order to promote agriculture and cooperate with the existing agricultural talents in Jiangsu Province, has specially opened a horticultural experimental field and a horticultural specialty school in Yu Tang Township, Shanghai. Technical personnel will be employed from the friends of Suzhou schools, and Liao Jianan (from Suzhou Agricultural School) will be invited to serve as principal to take charge of planning everything. It is scheduled to start on February 1st, 2020.

The General Situation of Suzhou's Banking Industry in 2019: Suzhou's banking industry has always had better profits than other industries at the end of each year's settlement. However, this year there is a significant downturn. The biggest reasons are: 1) Affected by the bankruptcy of peers in Yangzhou, Huzhou, and rice shops in the four rural areas, the losses amounted to 700,000 yuan, and all large and small peers were spared, especially the Qian Dazhuang, Sheng Da, in Guanqian, suffered the most. 2) Businesses in various industries are sluggish and the demand for funds is limited. On the one hand, due to competition among peers, most of the loans are with very low interest rates. At the end of the lunar year, due to the slow settlement, although the profit and loss cannot be determined yet, judging from the labor, even if there is a surplus, it is minimal. Many will offset profits and losses. Ruo Yuan is reported to be closing accounts next year, and there is also talk of Sheng Da closing accounts. In terms of new stores, it is heard that two small money shops have been opened, one named Hong Kang, with shareholders surnamed Guan and Xu, with a capital of 20,000 yuan. The manager is Bian from Shenghe. One is named Zhihe, with shareholders surnamed Zhang from Nanxiang, with a capital of 10,000 yuan. The manager is Li, formerly from Shengchang. The address is approximately in the eastern downtown area.

Jintan 69

Fa Du Town Robbed: The town of Sudu Pqiaotou, a few miles away from the city outside the Dadongmen of Fa Du Town, was suddenly attacked by a large gang of bandits at noon on the 23rd of this month. They first went to the Public Security Branch to rob guns and ammunition, and then surrounded the whole town, searching every household, none spared. At that time, the town chief, Yang, was working in the rural threshing floor and was notified by Cao, the principal of a certain elementary school in the town, and was able to avoid it. However, the bandits learned about the situation and shot and killed Cao. At the same time, a certain Jia was also shot and killed. About four or five people were injured. The total loss is estimated to be over 30,000 yuan. It is now heard that a certain Jia from the security regiment has contacted a certain group leader in the Huangjin Mountains and has some clues. Three bandits have been captured.

The Danger of Night Navigation in Tanben: Jintan's transportation is notoriously inconvenient. Usually, the traffic relies on Shaoxing-style fast boats to Benniu Town, connecting with the Beijing-Shanghai Railway line (it is relatively convenient to pass small wheels in summer due to the rising water). Because the villages and towns passed through are mostly in the territory of Danyang County, where Yuqiao Town is a central point that must be passed through for navigation. There have been incidents of robbery of express boats and travelers when they are more than ten miles away from the town. It is said that this has happened three times this year, especially when passing through the area in the dark.

Zhenjiang 70

General Situation of Chamber of Commerce Organizations in Various Counties: Chambers of commerce have been established legally in various counties of the province. They are organized by members of trade associations and shop members. According to the latest statistics, there are 13 counties including Zhenjiang, Danyang, Songjiang, Qingpu, Taicang, Jiading, Kunshan, Wuxi, Huaiyin, Jiangdu, Baoying, Tongshan, and Dangshan. As for the chambers of commerce in Yixing and Lianshui counties, because the trade associations of various industries have not been organized in advance, they must be reorganized according to law.

Large-Scale New Year's Amusement Fair: The Provincial Propaganda Committee is preparing to celebrate the 20th anniversary of the Republic of China on New Year's Day, which is extremely enthusiastic. In addition to holding lantern parades, etc., the amusement fair will be held in eight places, each with two performances. The first show will start at 5:00 pm on New Year's Day, and the second show will start at 8:00 pm. At 7:00 pm that night, fireworks will be set off in the sports field.

Mao Nijing's Corrupt Practices Case Judgement: Mao Nijing, the former director of the Dongtai Public Security Bureau, was transferred to the court for accepting bribes through his corrupt practices. After investigations and prosecutions, the case was publicly tried in court the other day. Yesterday, Judge Yang attended the court to announce the judgement. The main text announced was: Mao Nijing was sentenced to two years of fixed-term imprisonment for demanding bribes for acts in his official duties, fined 1,000 yuan, and deprived of his civil rights for five years. Pan Decai was sentenced to three months of fixed-term imprisonment for assisting in demanding bribes. Zhao Xiaozhou was found not guilty. It is heard that Mao was dissatisfied with the sentence and plans to appeal after receiving the verdict.

Yangzhou 71

Detective Team Arrests Fugitives: The Jiangdu County Detective Team, under the order of the county magistrate, was to strictly investigate and arrest the wanted bandits Wang Wengao (Wang Yugao), Chen Rong, Tongcai, etc. It is now learned that the team has arrested the bandits in Guocun, eastern part of the county. They also confessed to kidnapping a ticket in a certain place in July of this year and robbing a certain family in Tangjia Lane. Two boats were robbed outside the South Gate. Last night (29th) at 8:00, two ships moored under Baota Bay outside the South Gate of the city, the Wanlong button ship (loaded from Zhenjiang) carrying groceries, and Liu Shunqing's fishing boat, got over 50 dollars selling fish. Suddenly five bandits came, armed with box guns, and searched the ship. It was found that a gold ring and silverware, etc., were taken from Wan's ship. From Liu's ship, the money from selling fish, gold rings, cotton wadding, etc., were taken away. Wan et al. rushed to report to the merchants stationed there to pursue the bandits, but the bandits had already escaped far away.

Nantong 72

Sea Bandits Cause Trouble in Sanjia Town: After the two gangs of sea bandits, Pan Kaiwu and Shen Guanxi, fought each other, Shen bandit has now been wounded and killed. Pan bandit led more than 300 people and reoccupied Sanjia Town. He has been extorting huge sums of money from fishermen for days. If his wishes are not fulfilled, he will set fire to destroy ships. More than ten people have been abducted in Jiangnan. Only a Wusong merchant redeemed his life with 30,000 yuan. The merchants in the town are being forced by the bandits to supply food and fresh water on a daily basis. The disturbance is very serious. Residents of Pengjia District have already fled.

County Government Welcomes and Arrests Bandits: The Tongyi bandit Zhang Fengshan was captured in Shanghai. After being questioned by the Shanghai Special Zone Local Court, the Capturing Division sent a letter to the Nantong County Government, asking it to send police to welcome and arrest the bandit for investigation and handling. County Magistrate Zhang has sent police to welcome and arrest the bandit.

Celebration of the New Year by All Walks of Life: All walks of life in Nantong gathered at the Tongchong Haitai Chamber of Commerce on New Year's Day to hold a celebration meeting. In the afternoon, they jointly held an amusement fair. The business community closed for three days, all agencies stopped working for five days, and the press stopped publication for seven days.

The End of Local Cloth Industry in Tonghai: The local cloth industry in Nantong and Haimen counties has now ended. In 2019, the total amount of cloth made was 100,000 packages, and the total transaction amount was about 10 million yuan, which is only 60% of that in 2018.

Jiaxing 73

Hostage Redemption in Xinhuang: After the large gang of bandits robbed Xinhuang Town in southeast Jiaxing on the morning of the 23rd, they kidnapped 19 men, women, old and young when they left. It is now learned that the five shop clerks who were kidnapped have been released separately. Now, letters have been received from the bandits demanding ransom for Jiang Mousheng and Zhou Daguan, 100,000 for Jiang and 2,000 for Zhou. There is no news about the others. A Kidnapping Case Occurred in Cao Village, Yuxian: The house of Lin Xiaofang, a Ningbo overseas Chinese resident in Yuxian Town, Luoxiang Village, about three miles away, was robbed by bandits the other night, and Xiaofang was kidnapped. The chief of the sub-bureau in charge of the matter telegraphed the county government and the Public Security Bureau to request that a team be sent to suppress the bandits. Director Gao immediately sent Inspector Wang to lead the police brigade to the scene. When they walked to the head of Shabin, they learned that the bandits had already looted and left, so they returned to the city. Therefore, on the 30th, there was a false rumor in the city that Yuxian had been robbed. Also, the Tian Shun and Lu Hegui families, farmers near Cao Village, about seven miles away from Yuxian, were robbed at midnight the other night. The losses were quite large, and the case has been reported to the water and land police for investigation.

The Newly Appointed Minister to France 77

Qian Yongming's Talk

Going Abroad to Take Office After March or April

Going North to Handle Handover

The Successor to the Four Banks President is Undecided

The sixth State Council meeting of the Executive Yuan resolved to appoint Qian Yongming as the Minister to France, as seen in yesterday's newspaper. According to Qian Zi Xinzhi, he is a well-known figure in the banking industry. Qian is indeed the pioneer of bankers becoming diplomats. This newspaper's reporter specially visited Minister Qian yesterday to inquire about the date of his departure to France to take office. He replied that it would take a lot of time to handle the handover of the domestic banks and other businesses he was involved in, and that since Minister Gao Lu had not yet returned to China, he would not be able to go abroad until March or April. The reporter asked Qian Jun about the successor to the president of the Four Banks Savings Association, as Qian was the president of the association. Qian replied that it had not yet been decided, and that a board meeting would have to be convened soon to elect another person. Qian told the reporter that he planned to go to the north soon to handle the handover. Qian also told the reporter that he was very happy to have the opportunity to go abroad to observe after working in China for many years.

Sino-Egyptian Trade 78

Exchange of Notes Extending the Time Limit

Cancellation Should be Notified Three Months in Advance

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs that the Sino-Egyptian Trade Agreement had expired and requested that a remedy be found to extend the validity period of the exchange of notes. A telegram was sent to Minister Shi for verification, etc. A telegram was received from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, stating that the regulations regarding the end of the exchange of notes in the Sino-Egyptian Trade Measures of April 23 had been instructed by the Ministry to Minister Shi stationed in the UK on September 10 to consult with Egypt to amend or make a separate statement. Now, according to Minister Shi's reply, the Egyptian Minister has replied that the original exchange of notes has been changed to a long-term effective term without a three-month notice of cancellation. A written statement should be exchanged to show good faith, and a special reply will be sent for reference and notified to the Tobacco Industry Association. Ministry of Foreign Affairs Seal.

Local Autonomy Training Institute 79

Opening Ceremony Held Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal Government specially established a local autonomy training institute to train local autonomy personnel. The first batch of students in the institute, a total of 160 in the special class and 80 in the ordinary class, began classes on the 15th of this month and held a supplementary opening ceremony at 9:00 AM yesterday. The details are recorded below:

Participants: Zhang, the mayor, Yu, the director, You Bolu, the head of the Sixth District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Huang Daolin, the head of the Judicial Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Tang Naikang, the head of the Municipal Finance Bureau, Zhou Yongneng, the member of the Municipal Construction Discussion Committee, Su Xianyang, the salt transport envoy of Liangzhe, Wu Guangzong, the director of the Hydrographic Survey Bureau, Sun Baorong, the municipal government advisor, Zhang Taiji, the representative of the Garrison Headquarters, Wang Binyan, the organizing member of the Municipal Civil Defense Corps, Xu Peihuang, the head of the Education Bureau, Cen Dezhang, the secretary of the municipal government, Yao Yuanding, the representative of the local court, Ye Mujiu, the representative of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' office in Shanghai, and more than 300 students. The ceremony was presided over by Yu Hongjun, the director of the institute. Order of Ceremony: 1. Stand at attention. 2. Play music. 3. Sing the Party anthem. 4. Bow three times to the Party, the national flag, and the portrait of the President. 5. The chairman respectfully reads the President's will. 6. The mayor gives a speech. 7. Speech. 8. The director of the institute responds. 9. Play music. 10. Ceremony is completed. 11. Photograph. 12. Refreshments.

Mayor Zhang's Speech: This year, after the Central Legislative Yuan enacted the Municipal Organization Law in May, there was a basis for handling local autonomy. The city then established a district planning committee and a preparatory committee for the local autonomy training institute. The city has many talents, but it is not easy to carry out all local undertakings because they do not understand the special circumstances of the locality or the municipal government's administrative program. The establishment of this local autonomy training institute is therefore urgent. During the preparatory period of the institute, the qualifications and examinations of the students were carefully considered. "Students in the special class do not have to come to the institute due to economic limitations, but they can also receive the same training." Today, we have the opportunity to gather together to receive local autonomy training. How fortunate is this? If we can concentrate on studying what we have learned, we will be able to be competent and happy in serving the society in the future. There is also an incidental statement that students here do not need to ask whether they will have work after graduating in three months, but they should ask whether they have gained any insights during the study period. If they have excellent graduation results, they will not have to worry about society not welcoming them. I would like to briefly describe the essentials of training. The President's teachings show us that local autonomy is the foundation for implementing constitutional government. As for local politics in other countries, Germany is known for government rule, and the United Kingdom and the United States are known for civil rule, but each has its advantages and disadvantages. Our country had already handled local autonomy during the late Qing Dynasty, but the reason why it was not successful was that the handlers did not have appropriate methods, and scholars regarded it as a shortcut to becoming an official, which led to this. The so-called "training" is to use the foreknowledge to enlighten the latter, and the first knowledge to enlighten the latter knowledge, in order to cultivate the people's ability to use the four powers and increase the people's interest in participating in politics. The students here today are trained, and they will train people in the future, so they must pay special attention to their character and learning, cultivate their character and study hard, and prepare for the future. At the same time, it is especially important to pay attention to the word "practice." The ancients had the saying of practicing the heart, practicing the courage, and practicing the Qi. In short, the students' physical and mental training is very important. It is hoped that they will deeply understand and practice it.

Zhou Yongneng's speech: It is very pleasant to participate in the ceremony today. I heard that the teachers in this institute are all selected for a while. The results three months later will satisfy the students' wishes. It can be predicted that the Chinese Kuomintang wants to put the national politics on track, and the implementation of local autonomy is its first step. Such as population, land, transportation, roads, etc., are all local autonomy undertakings. Shanghai has achieved such results in a difficult environment of construction, which is not easy. New York in the United States has 400 million gold every year to manage municipal administration, and Chicago also has 300 million gold. How can it be as good as their achievements? If we want to do this immediately, it is of course impossible, but we can also plan at any time, the so-called first seek to have it, and then seek to be good. Only when the government's administration has measures, can the people assist. Judging from the spiritual aspect, for example, the government's investigation of the household registration is often not easy to obtain accurate answers. The fault is not entirely that the municipal government is not doing its job well, but that the people are not able to assist. Therefore, the people should always cooperate with the government, so that trouble can be avoided. You are here to study local autonomy, fortunately do not regard it as a thing of little importance. In addition to joy, I offer this tribute.

Director Yu's Response: It is an honor to receive Mayor Zhang's speech, Mr. Zhou Yongneng, the Construction Discussion Committee, and the presence of the guests today. I am very happy. This seat is under the command of the mayor, and is based on the central regulations, the municipal government's laws and regulations, and is in charge of the mayor's administration. Not only in this solemn ceremony, I am deeply frightened. Fortunately, you understand. Tracing back to the preparatory period of the institute, Mr. Huang Yisheng and Chen Dezheng have given a lot of support, especially Section Chief Huang's support for the most time. Mr. Ma Chong has planned in detail for teaching affairs. Mr. Chen Kecheng is cautious about moral education. Mr. Zhu Weikong has handled affairs properly. The spirit of the efforts of other colleagues has been very uplifting not long after the start of school. This can be gratifying to the mayor and guests. As for the future direction of the institute, in short, it is to cultivate the spirit of personal autonomy and cultivate the knowledge of personal autonomy in order to achieve the goal of local autonomy. In other words, to cultivate the spirit that individuals should have for autonomy, and to cultivate the knowledge that individuals should have for autonomy in order to achieve the ultimate goal of local autonomy. Now the unit of the national organization is the people. However, many people inevitably have excessive actions, that is, because they do not have sufficient knowledge. If individuals cannot be autonomous, society will not be on track, and the country will have no hope of perfection. Now the students have gathered here together to study, and I think they have already felt the importance of local autonomy. Therefore, on the one hand, I deeply hope to encourage each other, and on the other hand, I hope that the guests present will not hesitate to give guidance at any time to help me make up for my shortcomings.

The Decline of Shanghai's Shipping Industry Last Year 81

Most Chinese and Foreign Companies Suffered Losses

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Suddenly Greatly Improved

This year, gold is expensive and silver is cheap, and the import and export industry is the most depressed. The shipping industry has been affected by the war, the high price of hardware, the obstruction of transportation, and the decline in freight volume, which is worse than other industries. Almost all Chinese and foreign shipping companies on various rivers and seas in Shanghai this year have suffered heavy losses. Time flies, and another year has passed. The business conditions of various shipping companies in Shanghai are checked and reported as follows:

Taikoo Company: The British Taikoo Company has the most ships, and its routes cover the entire China, ranking first among the six companies. It has a total of 73 ships with a total of 163,000 tons. This year, the Yangtze River route was blocked due to the interruption of the Pinghan traffic and the disturbance of the Xiang-E bandits and communists. There were few imports and exports. The Sichuan River route was also caused by excessive competition and the indiscriminate drop in water feet. Although two new ships, Wuhu and Wuxue, were added to the Shanghai-Yichang route, the annual business has suffered a great loss. Within the North China route, only the regular three ships have slightly better business. The rest, such as the Andong and Yingkou routes, are also very deserted. On the Nanhua route, it is difficult to make a profit due to the lack of transshipment goods from the Yangtze River and North China. Only the newly added 12 ships on the Southeast Asia Islands route can make a profit because there are many overseas Chinese traveling to Fujian and Guangdong. The senior crew members of the company are mostly paid in gold pounds, and the secret losses this year are huge. Since September, the sailors have increased their wages, and the expenses have increased. The business losses this year are very huge. Fortunately, the capital is thick and the public accumulation is huge, so it does not matter much.

Jardine Matheson: Jardine Matheson has more than 40 ships with 120,000 tons. There are fewer ships in the Yangtze River class than Taikoo. This year, the business on the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River is only 40% or 50% of the previous year. After the Mingsheng ship was sold, the Binhe ship was added and the Shanghai-Yichang class was opened. The annual business is only on this route, and the loss is at least 700,000 or 800,000 yuan. There are 13 regular ships in the North and South Oceans. The Hakka people in the North Ocean helped the company to fine the water feet, and they allied to refuse to load goods, so the business was even more depressed and the losses were also very huge. At the moment, because of refusing to increase the salaries of the sailors, the sailors and firemen of each ship intend to deal with it by decisive means. The trade union is mediating, but I don't know how to solve it.

Nissin Kisen Kaisha: Nissin Kisen Kaisha specializes in the Yangtze River line, so the ships are the same as Taikoo. This year, the company's upstream and downstream business has special relations with the major yarn and cloth customs declaration firms in Shanghai, so it is unique in its loading. (One piece of yarn and cloth can be worth ten pieces of miscellaneous goods for water feet.) The losses are less. The business in the first half of the year was quite lost, and the business in the second half of the year only saw improvement in December. Statistics must also be lost. The four ships in the North and South Oceans are fortunate enough to break even.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company: Since the punitive military incident occurred, the ships of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company have been used for military purposes. The routes have been suspended one after another. Among the 25 ships in total, there were as many as 20 ships for difference. This year, the bureau was borrowing money to live on almost every day from January to August. After Zhao Tieqiao was assassinated, the situation in the bureau was at an unsustainable point, so Cai Pei and Chen Xizeng were unwilling to take over. Since Li Zhonggong came, he took on the dangerous situation despite all the difficulties and operated miserably. In the past four months, the business bureau, which was almost out of breath, has gradually moved towards a smooth path. The monthly expenditure of 300,000 can be paid out month by month without owing wages. After November, it took a further step to aggressively seek progress in the Yangtze River shipping industry. Shen Zhongyi in Shanghai and Li Yunliang in Hankou expanded the competition, and they can now leap over the six companies. The contribution of Shen and Li cannot be ignored. In the past, when the Yangtze River business of the bureau was the most prosperous, it was only 160,000 yuan a month, but now it can earn more than 200,000 yuan. However, there is only one ship on the upstream Yichang line, which is not enough to meet the demand. Li Zhonggong has decided to add four upstream oil-powered express ships for the development of Yichang and Hunan. The Nanhua route has also greatly improved in December. According to the current business (since November), the income of water feet on each route is enough to cover the expenses of the whole bureau. It is expected that according to the established steps in the spring, there will be a surplus. The new route in Southeast Asia is already in the process of chartering ships. Judging from the current business, according to the person in charge of the bureau, it is really an improvement that has not been seen since the Jiazi year.

Sanbei Company: Sanbei Company is the fastest-growing Chinese shipping company. It already has 18 river and sea commercial ships. It has been hit by wars for many years, and all coastal routes have been suspended. Only the Ningbo-Fujian and Yangtze River routes remain. This year, due to poor business, all the ships were leased for military use. At the same time, it also requested the issuance of 3 million yuan in sailing prices to add the Hongli and Hongzhen ships to expand the Yichang and Changsha classes, and built the Sanbei ship to operate the new route to Shenjiamen in eastern Zhejiang, which will soon be able to open. This year, the Yangtze River route has less losses. The sunken Feihu has already received 175,000 yuan in compensation from the headquarters. The Ningbo-Shanghai route, this year, the Ningxing ship has jumped to the top of the four ships.

Resolution of Labor Dispute Over Year-End Bonuses at a French-Owned Water and Electricity Company 85

Demand for Double Pay Led to a Half-Day Strike a Month Ago

Company Agrees to Graded Bonuses, Work Resumed Yesterday

The workers of a French-owned water and electricity company in this city held an emergency meeting at the labor union in Mingde Lane, Rue Lupan, on the 29th of last month. They resolved to demand a year-end bonus of one month's double pay for each person from the company. At 9:00 AM on the 30th, they appointed representatives, including Zhang Liansheng and five others, to make a direct request to Shen Shumei, the Chinese comprador of the French-owned water and electricity company in Lujiawan. Shen said, "This is a significant matter that I cannot resolve alone. I will discuss it with the manager, Meng Xiaolang (French), and then reply." By 12:00 noon, over 700 workers from the utility department held a mass meeting in the open space in front of the Lujiawan power plant. They resolved to go on a general strike at 1:00 PM that afternoon. The six representatives then negotiated with Compardor Shen and the manager. At 4:30 PM, the six representatives, including Zhang Liansheng, met with Compardor Shen. Shen stated that the manager wished the workers to resume work peacefully. Regarding the year-end bonus, it would be distributed according to years of service: (1) Those with two or more years of service would receive one month's double pay; (2) Those with one or more years of service would receive a bonus equivalent to seven-tenths of a month's wage; (3) Those with less than one year of service would receive a bonus equivalent to half a month's wage. However, the company's accounts for this year (i.e., last year) have already been finalized. The bonus funds would be distributed at 5:00 PM on the 31st (yesterday) and then added to the regular accounts. In the future, year-end bonuses would be distributed according to this precedent. The representatives deemed this satisfactory and reported back to the workers, who then fully resumed work yesterday morning. The over 700 workers in the transportation department did not participate in the strike. However, to ensure equal treatment, the company will also distribute bonuses to them according to the above precedent.

Opposition to the Auction of Stall Spaces in the Eight Immortals Bridge Market 86

Yesterday, a Petition Was Submitted to the Municipal Council… Hu Fangjin Appointed as Mediator

Small Vendors Organize a Group… Requesting Assistance from All Sides

The Eight Immortals Bridge Market in the French Concession has been under reconstruction for many months. All the vegetable vendors have been temporarily relocated to set up stalls in the open space in front of the Sino-French School to maintain their livelihoods. Now that the old market has been rebuilt with two stories, the vegetable vendors originally hoped to move back to their old locations after the market was completed and continue their business. However, yesterday's newspaper reported that the French Municipal Council would use an auction method to lease the stall spaces and stipulated eleven articles of regulations. The method involved an auction-style bidding, requiring annual bids in hopes of obtaining huge profits, resembling a stock exchange. Upon hearing this news, all the vegetable vendors panicked. They felt that this method would be unsustainable for small vendors who relied on meager capital for their livelihoods and would deprive them of their original right to occupy their stalls. Therefore, over 400 vegetable vendors collectively went to the French Municipal Council at the Big Bell Tower at 11:00 AM yesterday to stage a major petition. Upon witnessing the situation, the Western staff of the council were alarmed and immediately closed the doors. They also telegraphed the Big Bell Tower Police Station nearby to send officers to suppress the crowd. Concerned about their livelihoods, the vendors were unafraid and willing to face punishment. The police could not drive them away. Then, Mr. Hu Fangjin, the Chinese comprador of the council, came forward to mediate and offered heartfelt comfort to the vendors, saying, "The auction method was originally passed by the Municipal Council. Now that the vendors are concerned about their livelihoods, old stallholders can be allowed to bid first to show priority." However, the vendors unanimously expressed dissatisfaction and said that they would never agree to the auction of stall spaces. They asked Compardor Hu to appeal on behalf of the vendors and quickly propose a change to the Public Works Department. Mr. Hu agreed to find another solution and advised the vendors to disperse first. Knowing that Mr. Hu understood their hardships, the vendors followed his instructions and immediately dispersed. However, after leaving the Municipal Council, they regrouped in the temporary market in front of the Sino-French School and held a general meeting to discuss solutions. They elected 25 representatives to form the Eight Immortals Bridge Market Stallholders' Joint Association to present reasons and request assistance from the other side to achieve the goal of canceling the auction. At the same time, they will publish a translated declaration stating the reasons why they cannot bid. They will continue to petition the five Chinese directors and nine committee members of the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the French Concession to achieve their ultimate goal.

Wu Tingyu, Pan Jiazhen, and Dong Xihou
