China National Anti-Opium Society 89

Declaration Advocating Complete Opium Prohibition

The China National Anti-Opium Society issued a declaration stating: "The scourge of opium weakens the country and harms the people. After the National Government established Nanjing, the provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang initially adopted a policy of implicitly permitting opium by taxing it. However, they later followed public opinion and resolutely abolished it, adopting a policy of complete prohibition and establishing an Opium Prohibition Committee to demonstrate their determination. The people hoped that the international community would take this seriously, believing that the Opium Prohibition Committee, having been created by public opinion, would be able to effectively implement Dr. Sun Yat-sen's anti-opium teachings and realize the people's demand for opium prohibition. However, for the past two years, although the opium prohibition authorities have had plans to eliminate opium, they have lacked decisive and forceful action. Major cases such as officials transporting opium and warlords planting opium have occurred repeatedly, and most have ended inconclusively, causing social suspicion and international mockery. The situation has not improved. The planting of opium is still widespread in the northwest and southwest provinces, and even Anhui and Fujian are not exempt. Recently, southern Fujian has even faced a grain shortage crisis due to this. The forced planting of opium by the military has not stopped. Opium taxes are relied upon in Hunan and Hubei, and the sale of opium is openly conducted in Guangdong and Guangxi. Opium dens are scattered throughout the French Concession in Shanghai, and opium smuggling via Yangtze River steamers continues unabated, all becoming more rampant. This has only led to the people shouting and protesting themselves hoarse, without any effective measures being taken. Despite the nationwide struggle of the people over the past year, the results are disheartening. Now that the Fourth Plenary Session has been held, the government, following the resolutions, is preparing to vigorously enforce opium prohibition. Our society, which has always been dedicated to upholding Dr. Sun Yat-sen's anti-opium teachings and realizing the people's desire for opium prohibition, feels compelled to offer our humble suggestions to the authorities during this period of transition. Perhaps a foolish person's insights can help others polish their jade. We have observed that various countries around the world have adopted many methods for opium prohibition, but the opium prohibition policy is paramount. Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings have clearly shown us that the business of opium cannot coexist with the national government that is empowered by the people. Anyone who advocates for the legal permission of the opium business is an enemy of public opinion. He also said, 'Any responsible government agency that lowers its flag and ceases fighting against opium, regardless of the duration, is committing an act of selling out the country.' Furthermore, complete opium prohibition is stipulated in the Kuomintang's platform, and the policy of prohibition is also demanded by the entire nation. The National Government has the responsibility to uphold and implement it, and the obligation to develop and promote it. We sincerely hope that the authorities will embrace this principle and strive to implement it, not weakening due to obstacles or retreating due to difficulties. Although opium prohibition plans have been formulated over the years, in reality, the military protects and forces the planting of opium, and corrupt officials tax and condone opium trafficking, just as in the past. This is not the fault of the prohibition laws but rather the ineffective implementation of them. Recently, there have been calls to implement an opium monopoly to increase tax revenue, and it is rumored that this has already been agreed to by certain parties and will soon be implemented. Opium dealers are celebrating and eager to try it out. Our society firmly hopes that these rumors are false. However, there is no smoke without fire, and there is reason to believe that this is not entirely unfounded. Financial difficulties do not mean there are no other ways to raise funds. Why must we resort to opium, violating Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings, undermining the Kuomintang's platform, degrading our international standing, and destroying the opium prohibition treaties? Previously, when the League of Nations sent a Far East Investigation Team to investigate the opium situation, its purpose was to extend the opium monopoly policy to increase tax revenue. Our government and people were well aware of this and united to oppose it. Now, if we implement a monopoly ourselves, we would be taking over the previous opposition to foreigners profiting from opium trafficking to harm our people, and instead, killing our own compatriots. This would be tantamount to slapping ourselves in the face, which is extremely shameful. Today, the people's livelihoods are exhausted and industries are declining. We should seek ways to enrich the country and the people, not take poisonous measures to quench our thirst. The leaders of the party and the country are well aware of the people's suffering. At a time when internal conflicts have been resolved, it is an opportunity to start anew with the people. The laxity of opium prohibition is undeniable, and the difficulties in implementation are also real. Let the past be dead, and let the future be born. It is not too late to catch up and strive forward. Our society's responsibility lies in rejecting opium. Because of our deep concern, we cannot remain silent. Our hope for the National Government to eliminate opium is deep, and our words are also painful. Our society has no political color or factional purpose. Our statements come from sincerity. We hope that 1931 will be the year of the implementation of opium prohibition in our country. It will be fortunate for our compatriots and fortunate for our party and country."

Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Stipulates Docking Fees 90

Effective Today

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Notice No. 123 reads: "Regarding the matter of this bureau taking over and reorganizing the Nanshi docks, as ordered by the Municipal Government, a public notice has already been issued. The docking fee regulations previously established by the Port Authority for the Nanshi docks, specifically articles three and four, calculate docking fees based on the registered length of ships and use feet as the standard. Now, upon review of the Shanghai Municipal Unified Weights and Measures Regulations, it is stipulated that, starting from January of the twentieth year of the Republic of China, all official documents, correspondence, and various publications should uniformly adopt the metric system. The above-mentioned docking fees should be converted to meters for charging based on the original dimensions. However, to avoid complicated calculations with odd numbers, revised tables have been carefully considered and approved by the Municipal Government. These will be implemented starting January 1, 1931. This notice is hereby issued for public awareness."

Shanghai Municipal Nanshi Dock Docking Fee Calculation Table

Registered Length of Ship Docking Fee per Period per Meter

Meters Meters Yuan

30 to 45 0.60

45 to 60 0.66

60 to 75 0.72

75 to 90 0.78

90 and Above 0.84

For ships under 30 meters, the docking fee is 0.10 yuan per meter per use.

Establishment of Conciliation Office in Special District Court 95

For Civil Cases

All Kinds of Civil Cases

Will First Undergo Conciliation by Both Parties

If No Reconciliation is Possible

Then a Public Trial Will Be Held

The population of this city is increasing year by year and has now reached over three million. The increase is most noticeable in the International Settlement, which has led to greater commercial prosperity. However, as human affairs become increasingly complex, disputes over trivial matters naturally arise endlessly. As a result of these disputes, most end up in court. This is why the number of lawsuits in the Special District Local Court is increasing daily. However, once these types of civil cases are heard, the rights and wrongs are immediately clear, and there is no deep-seated animosity. If someone were to impartially mediate in advance, a resolution would likely be faster than a trial. Recognizing this, the court has established a civil case conciliation office. Starting this New Year's Day, all civil lawsuits will be first summoned to the court by the staff of the conciliation office. Without holding a formal hearing, they will inquire about the points of contention. Once the cause is clear, they will mediate between the two parties and persuade them to settle their dispute. If both parties respect the mediator's intentions, abandon the lawsuit, and express a willingness to reconcile, the mediator will facilitate a peaceful resolution. In the event that their opinions differ and there is no sincere intention to reconcile, or if the case cannot be resolved without legal intervention, the mediator will not force a reconciliation. Instead, a date will be set for a public trial. This method is newly created, takes into account both law and reason, and is beneficial and harmless. It is expected that once implemented, civil lawsuits will be greatly reduced. The location of the conciliation office has been designated by President Yang Zhaosun as the room next to the civil court. A sign for the conciliation office has been made and hung above the door of the room for public awareness.

The Mourning and Honors for Zhu Chengzhang 96

Over a Thousand Mourners at Yesterday's Interment

Three Institutions Fly Flags at Half-Mast in Mourning

The late banker Mr. Zhu Chengzhang's interment was held yesterday at 4 PM at the International Funeral Home. His remains were sent to the International Cemetery on Hongqiao Road for burial. Mr. Zhu had many friends during his lifetime, and yesterday, no fewer than a thousand people came to pay their respects and assist with the coffin. The plain carriages and white horses showed extreme honor and mourning. The deceased had served society for nearly twenty years, and the various enterprises he founded were quite remarkable. Moreover, he was always sincere in his dealings with others. His tragic and sudden death inevitably causes sorrow.

Names of Mourners: Those who attended the mourning and assisted with the coffin yesterday included Song Ziwen (represented by Song Ziliang), Qian Xinzhi, Huang Renzhi, Shen Enfu, Yang Dunfu, Yang Xianfen, Ou Weiguo, Zhuo Yongshi, Xi Jigeng, Fan Jimei, Fu Ruoyu, Pan Mingxin, Hu Jun'an, Xu Moude, Yan Deqing, Xia Xiaofang, Xu Xiuzhi, Hu Xuanming, Liu Zhan'en, Wang Boheng, Liu Hongsheng, Fan Zhigui, Zhuang Dezhi, Zou Bingwen, Xu Jiqing, Li Fusun, Wu Yunzhai, Qu Yingguang, Xia Juchuan, Lin Kanghou, Shou Jingwei, Diao Xinde, Chen Shiguang, Li Moxi, and Western guests, as well as all staff members of the National Goods Bank, Shanghai Bank, and China Travel Service, totaling over a thousand people. They were all received by Mr. Zhu's younger brother, Chenghou, and relatives Huang Hongdao and his brothers. Yesterday, the National Goods Bank, Shanghai Bank, and China Travel Service all flew flags at half-mast to show their deep mourning. The traffic on Jiaozhou Road was so congested that it almost became impassable. The Jing'an Temple Road police station dispatched many Chinese and foreign detectives to direct traffic and take care of everything.

The Interment Ceremony: Mr. Zhu's remains were moved from the upstairs to the downstairs hall at 4 PM. The mourners waited in silence, and all who saw the coffin were saddened. Then, Pastor Zhu Baoyuan led the congregation in singing hymns. The mournful sound was mixed with sighs. Dr. Yu Rizhang gave a speech before the coffin, stating that everyone deeply regretted Mr. Zhu Chengzhang's tragic death. However, his short life and contributions to society were already very obvious. If Heaven had granted him a longer life, his achievements would have been even more immeasurable. Mr. Zhu's success was due to his great personality and sound virtues. Although his physical body has withered, his spirit will endure forever, serving as an example for us all.

Many Assisted with the Coffin: After the interment, the coffin was transported to the International Cemetery on Hongqiao Road. The mourners proceeded with the coffin under the bleak sky, and the scene was very solemn. Behind the hearse, there were hundreds of vehicles following the procession. The wreaths that filled the hall were also transported to the cemetery and piled at the tomb.

Condolence Telegrams: After Mr. Zhu's death, many condolence telegrams were received from various parties. (1) The Telegraph Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs telegraphed: "To Brother Xie Wentong, we were shocked to hear of your uncle's passing. We are deeply saddened. We hope you will cope with the changes and take care of yourself. We send our condolences. From all colleagues of the Telegraph Department." (2) Cui Renlin telegraphed: "To Mr. Xie, 189 Yuyuan Road, transfer to Mrs. Zhu. The sad news has arrived, and we are deeply saddened." (3) The owner of the Da Lai Company, Robert Dolla, in San Francisco, was deeply saddened by the news of Mr. Zhu's death and also sent a telegram of condolence yesterday.

Memorial Meeting: The local National Young Men's Christian Association, as Mr. Zhu was a Christian and chairman of the YMCA, the General Affairs Department of the association has sent letters to the 92 directors, including Wang Zhengting, Zhang Zhijiang, and Kong Xiangxi, to hold a memorial service in early this month.

Nineteen Men and Women Kidnapped

Beside the Zhenru Railway 98

Tragically Murdered Male Corpse

The Deceased Appears to be a Gangster

The Cause of Death is Suspected to be a Revenge Killing

A tragic assassination occurred in the fields beside the Yangjia Bridge railway tracks at the Zhenru Station of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway. The circumstances are investigated and recorded below:

Elegantly Dressed Male Corpse: Yangjia Bridge is located in a remote area, rarely visited, especially at night. The day before yesterday (the 30th), a villager going to market saw a well-dressed man who had been shot to death, covered in blood. The blood was still fresh. He was shocked and shouted loudly. The patrol police from the Third Section of the Fourth District learned of this and, after investigation, reported it to the station. They began an investigation but did not know his name. They ordered the local bailiff to report the verification.

Multiple Gunshot Wounds on the Body: In the afternoon, after the bailiff reported the verification to the Local Court, the prosecutor Wu Shixin, accompanied by the examiner Xuan Zhiming and clerks and bailiffs, rushed to the scene by car. The corpse was found to be about 30 years old, wearing a silk-lined velvet long gown, gabardine lined jacket and trousers, a woolen short shirt, a sanitary undershirt, woolen socks, dark green leggings, black velvet shoes, and a new-style long overcoat of reddish-purple Mackintosh. The name "Xing Youling" was attached to the coat pocket, presumably the name of the deceased. However, the deceased had a shaved head (due to ringworm) and was wearing a wig. As for the wounds, one gunshot entered the forehead and exited the back of the head. Another bullet entered below the right ear and did not penetrate. Two gunshots to the abdomen also did not penetrate. It was determined that the death was caused by the wounds. The post-mortem report was filled out, photographs were taken, and the body was taken to the mortuary, awaiting identification and arrest of the murderer.

The Deceased Resembles Xing ErMao: The deceased was of medium build and very thin. It is said that the person looked like Xing ErMao, because ErMao was bald and wore a wig. His name was also Youling. He lived at the Hanqiao of the North Railway Station and had no occupation, that is, what Shanghai people call a gangster. Therefore, this case is determined to be a revenge killing. The court has sent police to investigate the family.

The Bizarre Divorce Case of the Wife of a Cook at Da San Yuan 99

How Can a Husband Connive at Another Man's Adultery with His Wife?

Ms. Yang Accuses Her Husband of Having a Hidden Illness

The Sister-in-Law Acts as the Husband

The Cook Boasts That He Can Fulfill His Duties

The Judge Orders a Medical Examination for Further Review

Hu Guanfu, a cook at the Da San Yuan Restaurant, is from the Hua Jing Township of Longhua. He has some property. On November 5th of the sixteenth year, he married Ms. Yang, who was from the same village. They initially lived in the countryside for about two months. Later, Hu was employed in the concession and lived far from home, making it inconvenient to return. So, he moved his wife to the concession. He left early and returned late. On December 16th of the eighteenth year, Ms. Yang suddenly disappeared. She returned in March of the following year, insisting that Hu take her back to the countryside. But on the day they were supposed to return, she disappeared again. In July, they met at Zhaofeng Garden. Hu saw that her abdomen was as big as a five-stone gourd, and he knew that she had been unfaithful. They argued, and afterward, Ms. Yang hired a lawyer to file for divorce in the Special District Court. She claimed that Hu had only spent forty yuan on the engagement gift, while her dowry was worth more than two hundred yuan. Not long after the wedding, Hu admitted to having a hidden illness, and because the family was poor, Hu's sister, Wang, accompanied her to work at the Shenxin Yarn Factory and lived at her sister's house. As a result, she was raped by her brother-in-law, Shi Xuetang. Wang told her that Hu could not have sexual relations because of his illness and asked him to

Act as Husband to Ensure Offspring and Prevent Extinction. She Promised That Her Life Would Be Maintained by Shi. She, A Weak Woman, Could Not Resist, and Was Seduced by Flattery, Leading To Defilement. Afterward, She Lived With Wang In Several Places. Hu Knew But Did Not Speak. This Shows That His Hidden Illness and Entrusting Her Sister-In-Law To Act As Husband Are Real. Over Time, Hu's Sister Wang Became Jealous And Conspired With Hu To Deceive Her Into Going To The French Concession, Intending To Sell Her. She Saw Through This And Called Out. Last January, She Was Lured To Shanghai By Wang Yuntang And Lived With Him For Six Or Seven Months, Then Was Abandoned, Without A Means Of Survival. She Returned To Her Ex-Husband, Who Ignored Her.

The Pregnancy Resulting From The Rape Has Now Led To Childbirth, Further Worsening Her Plight. Hu And His Sister And Brother-In-Law Conspired To Abuse Her, Starting With Affection And Ending With Abandonment. Jiang Youzhi Makes Demands of Dong Yu 101

Totaling Three Points

The divorce case of lawyer Dong Yu, who sued his wife Jiang Youzhi for divorce, failed to be resolved. Jiang has now applied for assistance from the Municipal Women's Association. It is reported that the Women's Association has accepted the petition and is preparing to forward it to the French Concession Court for a fair judgment. Jiang's demands are as follows: (1) If they live together, improve the treatment and do not continue to live in the pavilion, with a repelling attitude, worse than that of a maidservant. (2) If they live separately, prepare adequate living expenses and expenses for the daughter's marriage when she grows up, which must be effectively guaranteed and not just empty words that cannot be obtained. (3) In order for Dong Yu to fulfill one of these two demands, Youzhi allows him to marry anyone, sacrifices everything, and will never interfere, and signs documents as evidence. It is said that Wu Tianni, Jiang's maternal grandfather, recently conveyed that if the lawsuit is won, she should enjoy the rights of the judgment. She (referring to Youzhi) does not want to accept the condition of 3,000 yuan in interest-bearing alimony, and the marriage expenses must be returned, which is her own fault. If the lawsuit is lost, she will file another lawsuit for cohabitation, requesting cohabitation and improved treatment in the pavilion, which goes without saying. But her ability cannot control one Ms. Lu, and if I marry someone stronger than Ms. Lu, and the two of them live together, let's see what her ability is. The implication is nothing more than a demonstration of a final break.

Fourteen Small Newspaper Offices 102

Misunderstanding with Zhan Jifeng Resolved

It is reported that the misunderstanding between the fourteen small newspaper offices and lawyer Zhan Jifeng has been resolved, and they are back on good terms. The exchange of letters between the two parties is recorded below:

Letter from Zhan Jifeng to the Various Small Newspaper Offices: Gentlemen, in the case of Ms. Hu Die suing Lu Yifang, editor of the Ling Bao, in the Shanghai Special District Court for defamation, when I stated in court, I only said, "This is not a flyer, but something published in a newspaper. Even if it is a contribution, the editor should be responsible," and did not say anything about this type of flyer-like newspaper engaging in deceptive practices. There is a court transcript that cannot be arbitrarily deleted or altered. I have many literary friends in the small newspaper industry, and insulting literary friends is tantamount to insulting myself. I am not so foolish as to do this. This record is clearly a misunderstanding based on hearsay or deliberately exaggerated by interested parties to provoke discord. I fear that the misunderstanding will spread further, so I hereby correct it. Furthermore, I am always in favor of peace. Even in this case with Ling Bao, I wrote a letter in advance to advise them to make sincere corrections, but unfortunately, they were not accepted. Instead, they made insincere corrections and published a satirical piece in the next issue, which provoked the lawsuit and could not be stopped. This is my difficult but unappreciated effort to mediate in advance, so I cannot remain silent. Please lend your newspaper space to publish this humble letter. I would be grateful for your cooperation. Sincerely, To: Da Bao Guan, Zhengqi Bao Guan, Jingangzuan Bao Guan, Shanghai Bao Guan, Taiyang Bao Guan, Tie Bao Guan, Ling Bao Guan, Ping Bao Guan, Holmes Bao Guan, Dajing Bao Guan, Shanghai Luo Bao Guan, Clays Bao Guan, Shehui Ribao Guan, Huang Bao Guan.

Letter from Various Newspaper Offices to Zhan Jifeng: Sir, we have received your letter and understand that it was a misunderstanding. Now that we have clarified the matter, we should shake hands as before. The letter we previously consulted you about is hereby withdrawn. This is a reply to Lawyer Zhan Jifeng.

National Arts Groups Welcome Chu Minyi 103

Shanghai National Arts Municipal National Examination Association, Shanghai YMCA, Shanghai Wuxue Association, etc., welcomed Mr. Chu Minyi at the YMCA conference room at 3 PM yesterday. Those present included Li Zibi of the YMCA's Sports Department, Zhao Daoxin of the Shanghai Wuxue Association's First Department, Zhang Changxin of the Second Department, Tong Zhongyi of the Municipal National Arts Hall, Liu Desheng of the Public Sports Ground, Bao Gang of the Association, Yao Fuchun of the Zhongshan Wuxue Association, Zhang Keming of Shanghai Public School, Weng Deqin of Minfu School, as well as Ge Gongzhen, Qian Yantang, Cai Xiangsun, and YMCA Sports Secretary Ling Xitao, totaling more than forty people. Weng Guodong presided over the meeting, Wu Yuren recorded the minutes. After the formalities, a welcoming speech was delivered. Mr. Chu said that in terms of sports, hygiene, diplomacy, education, and other aspects, we can all learn from him. In terms of national arts, he invented the Tai Chi ball and physical fitness testing equipment, which are all admirable. He has returned home with honor from participating in the World Expo. People in our national arts community should welcome him sincerely and hope that colleagues will unite and break down barriers to develop in a systematic way in the future. Then, Chu Min delivered a speech, saying that he was both grateful and ashamed to receive the welcome from his national arts colleagues. As the chairman said, this is what he hopes for. In the future, he hopes that everyone will recognize that the purpose of practicing national arts is for health, use simple methods to create universal talent, and use indirect testing methods as a competition tool to promote the progress of national arts. He also invented a simple method for Tai Chi exercises, which he demonstrated on the spot. Then, Ge Gongzhen said that sports is something that he likes, but he regrets that busy people cannot do what they want. Therefore, he hopes that national arts will have opportunities for busy people to practice and advocates for a health certificate. If the staff of various institutions do not have this certificate, they can be refused employment, which can achieve universal results. Then, Yao Fuchun and others made speeches. Then refreshments were served and the meeting adjourned.

Gold Firm Manager 104

Embezzlement of Huge Sums Case Rescheduled for Hearing

Shi Yulin, manager of Yong Sheng Chang Gold Firm, Huang Hongxuan, the accountant, and Shi Xianglin, the runner, colluded to defraud the accounts and embezzle the huge sum of 173,250.222 taels of silver. It is really the largest case of embezzlement by commercial employees in recent years. After Shi and others were sued by shareholders Gu Yuanruo, Wang Boyuan, Wu Shanqing, and You Xianghe, who hired three lawyers Wang Fuchang, Chen Zhongyin, and Tao Wuzhi to the Special District Court, they were arrested by the police. People in the gold industry regarded it as a major case, unprecedented. Each time the trial was held, many people came to listen. The day before yesterday afternoon, when Judge Zhou Hanting continued the hearing, the audience was still full. The defendants hired lawyers Chen Tingrui and Chen Ying to defend them. First, lawyer Chen Tingrui spoke, saying that the plaintiff's indictment listed twelve charges of criminal facts against the defendant, all of which were general terms and did not state who committed what crime. Moreover, the situation in the gold industry is complex, and the details are not known to outsiders. The plaintiff should be ordered to submit all the books and documents to the Gold Industry Association for detailed investigation or clarification, otherwise, it would be difficult for the defendant to answer. For example, the twelfth charge against him is the entanglement of the 4,000 yuan deposit in the Jin Cheng Bank, which is actually a misunderstanding. If the defendant has enough time, he will be able to prove each item. Lawyer Chen Ying continued by saying that the gold industry transactions have neither goods nor cash, like gambling, which is actually speculation. Gambling should be illegal. The judge should order the police lawyer to file a lawsuit against the plaintiff for making speculation a regular business. If the police do not want to sue, then please ask the prosecutor to exercise the power of indictment so that speculation can be reduced. Judge Zhou said that this was another matter and had nothing to do with this case, and ordered the lawyer not to mix it up, but to debate the case according to the law, so as not to cause complications. Then the defendant's lawyer requested a postponement to prepare the defense. The court granted the request and ordered the defendants to be returned to custody for another hearing in fourteen days.

Recent Events of the Tobacco and Exchange Industry Association 108

The Municipal Tobacco and Exchange Industry Association has extended the deadline for the spring license tax for tobacco and alcohol due to the National New Year. Yesterday, it specially notified the industry that the case was investigated. The period from January 1st to 10th of the 20th year is the period for renewing the spring licenses. The association informed the Second District Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Collection Office yesterday that the agency is on holiday for several days at the beginning of the National New Year and inquired about the start date and extension deadline of the letter. The letter stated that the period for renewing the spring tobacco and alcohol license tax for the 20th year is limited to January 1st to 10th. However, according to recent reports, all agencies will be on holiday for four days at the beginning of the National New Year. During this period, will your office stop collecting taxes, or will it start collecting taxes on January 5th and extend the deadline to January 14th? We should consult and reply so that we can notify our industry to renew the new spring license within the time limit so that both the tax and the business will suffer no losses. After sending it to the office, the office replied that all agencies have been on holiday for four days at the beginning of the National New Year, and our office should also comply with the order, from the 31st of this month to the 3rd of January of the 20th year, suspend the collection for four days, and set it to open on January 4th and extend the deadline to January 13th. The letter should be checked and all the treasure shops that should be renewed for the spring tobacco and alcohol licenses must go to renew them from January 4th to 13th, within ten days, and must not be overdue to be fined. This is the most important special notice and also to propose the case of cutting the li tax. The Shanghai South Office continued to send a letter to the Executive Committee stating, "Gentlemen, we have received a letter from the Soy Sauce and Alcohol Industry Association stating that we have received a public letter from your association stating that the three opinions submitted by our association a few days ago have been accepted by your Executive Committee, and we have convened a joint discussion to facilitate the launch, etc. Because of this matter, our association should convene the Executive Committee to send representatives, but it cannot be held because of the hasty end of the year. Moreover, Chairman Zhang is going to Beijing on official business and must return to Shanghai in early January. Fortunately, it is a matter of concern to the two industries of your industry. Our association asks ourselves to have a spirit of struggle and not to fall behind. After your association proposed it, our association should follow the lead and not shirk its responsibility. It is a matter of course to work hard and carry it out. This is the case, and the office should check it and carry out the work with perseverance and without fear." The office had previously reported that the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee had resolved to implement the new business tax after the li tax was changed, and that similar fee taxes such as the state-run sales of tobacco and alcohol and tobacco and alcohol licenses should be abolished to conform to the system and reduce the burden. The opinion was proposed and sent to the Executive Committee, and the original text was sent to the Soy Sauce and Alcohol Industry Association to seek consent. Subsequently, the association approved a letter of reply, including three opinions, and then our office sent a letter to your association for review and implementation. It was decided by your association at the 14th Executive Committee meeting on the 23rd to first urge the Soy Sauce and Alcohol Industry Association to hold a joint meeting on a regular basis, and then jointly send letters to the relevant industry associations to solicit comrades. The office was asked to send invitations to the cases on file, and the letter stated the cause and sent a letter to the Executive Committee Chairman Chen to check it and carry out the work with perseverance.

Free Talk Congratulations

New Year's Free Talk Zhou Shoujuan Conghe

Apologies for not sending separate invitations

Twenty New Year's Day Spring Lantern Ode · Cheng · Zhan · Lu

Heaven opens civilization. No one. Disobeys. Benefiting these people is not necessary to divine. Having sheathed our bows. Enjoying ourselves with cups. Completing the revolution. Cheering with hats off. Auspicious atmosphere throughout the sky. More than enough. Heaven minus man is two. Down minus divination and drawing minus bow. Combine to make ten. Complete minus hat is Yuan. Throughout minus one is Dan. The ode hides the four characters "Twenty New Year's Day".

Retrospect and Hope for New Year's Day Zhang Mengzhao

Pepper platters offer the year, cypress wine welcomes spring. Is this not the New Year's Day festival? Today, announcing the new moon and offering sheep. Following the national calendar. Treading this new year. Reminding of the past and looking to the future. Cannot be without words. Retrospecting since the founding of the Republic of China. As far as memory goes. The overthrow of autocracy in the first year of the Republic of China. Establishing a democratic polity. And Father of the Nation Sun Yat-sen. Was elected as the first president. The national jubilation on New Year's Day. Was the most enthusiastic. Afterwards, the government moved north. Xiangcheng defied the world's disapproval. Presumptuously proclaimed himself emperor. Eventually, the martyr Cai Songpo rose up in anger and abolished it. After the era of Hejian, Huangpi, Donghai Zhongshan, and Hefei. No year went without cyclical warfare. Getting worse every year. Not to mention the bleak New Year's Day. Even National Day was a bitter smile. In the spring of the sixteenth year. The revolution succeeded. The government moved south. Thus, the atmosphere was renewed. The whole country celebrated. Now, the north and south have joined hands. The unification is consolidated. Is this not a phoenix singing towards the sun? A happy phenomenon of coming from adversity? While we celebrate the National New Year's Day with joy and excitement. Our only hope. Is to wish the government sound. The country permanently unified. As long as the evergreen pine and cypress. As radiant as the sun and moon.

Precious New Year's Auspicious Words Liu Mei Ju

The National New Year. Strictly enforced from the beginning. Those who serve in political life. Live in this era. Be people of this era. Their auspicious words supporting the new initiatives. Are certainly all out of sincerity. As for others, such as the position of all circles under the blue sky and white sun flag. Having known that political orders are renewed. And not being reactionary elements. They also dare not not celebrate this New Year. Adding auspicious words. However, the auspicious words I have recorded. Do not overly exaggerate things. Nor completely beautify. Street talk and gossip. Women's words and children's sayings. This is certainly true public opinion. It can also be seen that our compatriots. Are rich in faith. Although the imperial system has been extinguished. But the thought of "comfort me as a ruler" is everywhere. Therefore, I am happy to record it. As something precious.

Auspicious Words from Naughty Children's Mouths Yesterday, I took a Route 1 tram to Hongkou. At the Risheng Building station. There was a six- or seven-year-old child. Who got on the bus with his parents. Sitting and standing restlessly. Sometimes peering outside the bus. Sometimes stepping on the shoes and socks of people on the bus. At a glance, one could tell he was a naughty child. However, when he heard people on the bus talking about the National New Year. He was very happy. Holding his mother's neck, he laughed and said. Good, good. The old calendar has leap months. Hoping for the New Year is as difficult as ascending to heaven. But now and hereafter. The New Year will really come easily.

New Character Prediction Zhu Zhu

Recently, at Old Muddlehead's place. I saw him predicting the two characters "Revolution". What he said made the general public. Hear and be encouraged. Therefore, I recorded it. As a New Year's Day wish for the twentieth year.

The character "革" (Ge, Revolution) is analyzed. Can be separated into the three characters "廿" (Nian, Twenty) "中" (Zhong, China) "一" (Yi, One). Meaning that after "Twenty" years. The National Revolution of "China's" people. Can be counted as truly "united".

The character "命" (Ming, Life/Fate/Command) is analyzed. Can be separated into the three characters "人" (Ren, People) "一" (Yi, One) "叨" (Dao, to receive favor). Meaning that the "People" of China. After twenty years. Can all "receive" "all" benefits.

New Drinking Game · Zhan · One · Smile

National New Year. Gathering around the stove to drink. For a dinner gathering of three people, A, B, and C. A new drinking game is played. Each person must say a four-character idiom that secretly relates to the twentieth year. Otherwise, they will be fined a large cup of wine. Everyone agreed. First, C was recommended. C said, "Four Cardinal Principles and Five Constant Virtues." Next was B. B said, "Crowning begins with learning etiquette." Finally, A said, "Upon reaching adulthood, one is given a courtesy name." Thus, everyone raised their glasses to congratulate.

The words were extremely unintentional. However, the girdle and finger guard. Are included in the Odes. Although the child is naughty. He is innocent. Therefore, it is ordered as the first auspicious word.

Auspicious Words from the Jealous Wife in the Boudoir. Last Monday. I attended a friend's birthday banquet. I heard a fun story from a guest. A guest had a relative, Mr. Zhao. Who lived with one wife and one concubine. They usually got along very well. And there were no quarrels. Recently, the wife suddenly said to her husband. The country has already adopted the Gregorian calendar. The expenses of all agencies have been revised. Our family should also comply. The husband also presented himself in the village autonomy. And happily agreed. Thus, the monthly allowance that you give each month. Will also be changed from the National Calendar from the New Year's Day of the twentieth year. Although this is using public office for private purposes to carry out her jealousy. However, the country's political orders. Extend to the boudoir. Therefore, it is ordered as the second auspicious word.

Auspicious Words from an Ignorant Teacher An ignorant teacher is in a precarious situation today. And will perish along with the old calendar. There is a Mr. Qu. Still using "Zhihu Zheye" (classical Chinese particles). Begging for food at the home of a wealthy household in a certain village in Suzhou. Hearing people say that the change of calendar is inconvenient for farming families. He said sternly. The sages of the Three Dynasties. And the tyranny of the Qin Dynasty. Changing the year and issuing calendars. The people all followed. Now, changing the calendar is also a story of everyone participating in the new. Why are there so many arguments? This was also told by a guest at the banquet. Although this kind of ignorant person is not appropriate in ethics. He also knows to follow orders. And can cite historical events. Among the ignorant, he is still better than others. Therefore, it is ordered as the third auspicious word.

New Year's New Game Qiushui

With the sound of firecrackers dispelling the old, today is New Year's Day of the 20th year of the Republic of China. Little brothers and sisters have nothing to do at home. I would like to offer a few new games as follows. Practice it on the spot. To entertain oneself. And to entertain others.

Although the new "Crossing Five Passes" game is a small game. It is not worth taking if it lacks profound meaning and strong interest. Old-style games. Although there are those that meet these conditions. But people get tired of them over time. It is human nature. Therefore, based on personal opinions and experiences. I will describe a new game of "Crossing Five Passes". The method is to first gather many people, big and small, male and female. Arrange chairs in rows facing each other. Leaving a considerable gap in the middle. The distance is such that the toes of those sitting opposite each other can touch. Once seated. Everyone touches each other's feet. Then choose two people (preferably one male and one female) to cover their eyes with towels. Order them to take steps forward. When those sitting see them walking. They gently withdraw their feet. The space between the two rows of people. Has suddenly become a wide road. But the blindfolded people do not know. And are still restrained. Unable to move an inch. The actions of the two people. Are very funny. If the blindfolded person knows that their feet have been withdrawn. When walking forward slowly. Those sitting in front. May as well stretch out their feet again. To make them somersault once. Or make a gold ingot shape. That would also be very fun. According to the process of life. There are many obstacles and dangers. If one is not careful in handling things. One cannot avoid falling. Those who engage in this kind of game. May be able to understand the true meaning of life from this.

Game Court The spirit of a country ruled by law. Lies in the ability of the people to understand the law. Legal education. Therefore, it must be promoted and popularized. The game court. Is one of the new games invented by me. Imparting legal knowledge through games. I think it will also be taken by those who know. When guests gather together. And the interest in chatting gradually fades. The game court can be held. First, ask a guest to voluntarily leave the seat. Once they are out. Then choose someone to be the judge. Sitting high in the courtroom. The guests then stand up one by one. Accusing the crimes of the person who left the seat. May as well use all kinds of tricks. And be as funny as possible. The judge takes notes. And records the names of the accusers. Once finished. Summon the person who left the seat. Tell them what happened. Ask them who accused them. If the accused guesses correctly. They will be released. And the person who was guessed correctly will replace them. The guest at the seat suddenly becomes a prisoner. That is also fun.

Today's Xie Gongzhan Individual Works Exhibition He Tianjian

Mr. Xie Gongzhan is one of the most ethical people in our painting circles. He has a long-standing reputation and his paintings are worth a lot of money. Now, on New Year's Day of the twentieth year of the Republic of China. He is holding an individual works exhibition on the third floor of the Ningbo Fellow Association. The meaning of this exhibition. I heard is to fulfill the agreement with his younger brother, Mr. Jiezhi, who died, and to commemorate him. Because the two brothers. Competed in playing the xun and chi (ancient Chinese wind instruments). And were known as Jiyuan at the time. And Mr. Jiezhi was especially good at writing lyrics. Whenever his elder brother completed a painting. He would write a clear poem on it as an embellishment. Which was spread as a good story in the art world. In recent years, Mr. Jiezhi felt that the trend of society. Was gradually leaning towards art. He strongly encouraged Mr. Xie to exhibit his lifetime works. To promote it. But Mr. Xie was dedicated to painting. And was always busy. And did not agree. Until Mr. Jiezhi died of illness this autumn. At the time of his death. He persuaded him again. And Mr. Xie was greatly moved. And his friends and relatives told him that Mr. Xie was crying for his brother day and night. And was about to get sick. They all advised Mr. Xie to quickly fulfill his brother's agreement. To engage in painting. Which could comfort the heart of the deceased and also dispel grief. Thus, this grand exhibition. With one hundred and seventy or eighty famous works. Was produced in this short period. Mr. Xie painted until late at night. Sometimes he even stayed up all night. Ink marks and lamp shadows. Often revealed spiritual realms. Pond spring grass. Came divinely from under his brush. There must be a reason for this. It is also heard that the works for this exhibition. Were originally set at one hundred and fifty pieces. But the number that has been ordered. Has exceeded the original amount and reached more than one hundred and eighty pieces. This shows the eagerness of the social people to admire Mr. Xie's works. However, the fairground must give people a new opportunity.

New Year's Literary Riddles · Wu · Lian · Zhou

Congratulations on the New Year (a sentence from the Four Books)

Implement the national calendar and abolish the old calendar (a sentence in classical Chinese)

Honest and virtuous (a sentence from Five-character Tang poetry)

A feather in the vast sky (a sentence from the Western Chamber)

Green lush and red faded (a Beijing opera name)

Old master of Cangshan (a character)

Having the same beauty, people all raise their heads and look at it (a contemporary person's name)

How deep or shallow is the painted eyebrow, is it fashionable (a sentence from Seven-character Tang poetry)

Heaven rains gold (a sentence from the Book of Songs)

Legacy not forgotten, following Jingjie (two county names in Zhejiang Province)

Dividing the Luo Village equally horizontally (a Ci melody name)

Writing without adding dots (a sentence from the Three Character Classic)

The above literary riddles are casually picked. To help the gentlemen who read the newspaper during the New Year to have some fun. If you are interested in submitting answers. Please send them to Wu Yi's residence next door to this newspaper before the tenth. I have prepared a small reward. To answer your elegant intentions. There is also a newly reformed literary riddle bi-monthly publication. The writers are all famous writers in Shanghai. Send five cents for postage and it will be mailed.

Therefore, a method was agreed upon. All those who have a fixed price will be calculated at 20% off. To give preferential treatment to visitors. I passed by Mr. Xie's residence a few days ago. And was shown his famous works. All of which were carefully crafted. No wonder the exhibition has not yet been held and the works have already been ordered.

(In response to reward) Carrying on the Family Tradition Cao Mengyu

Four years ago. Under the lush and verdant Huanghuagang. There was often a haggard-looking man. Loitering and not leaving. Often until the sun set in the west. And the smoke from cooking began to rise. People still saw him lingering at the foot of the hill. As if there was something beautiful. Enough to hold his heart. And make him reluctant to leave. In fact, there was nothing fun about that hill. Few people usually went there. And no one regarded this hill as a scenic spot. So it was usually very quiet. Only this haggard-looking man was often seen.

Later, I met Chen Buping several times. And gradually became acquainted. Only then did I know that although he looked haggard. And seemed to be in his thirties or forties. In reality, he was very young. Only just over twenty years old. Chen Buping lived near Huanghuagang. After we became acquainted. I often invited him to sit at home. Because the two of us had similar interests. And our conversations were very congenial. Moreover, he was the son of Mr. Xiong, one of the seventy-two martyrs who were buried under Huanghuagang. His name was Xiong Ye. Buping greatly respected the seventy-two martyrs. So he loved the crow on the roof. And also valued Xiong Ye. But although our conversations were congenial. Xiong Ye refused to talk about his situation and purpose. The detailed history of the seventy-two martyrs is not clear to the world. Especially since Mr. Xiong's name is not even known to the world. Chen Buping asked Xiong Ye. But he did not say. Only talked about things that were not directly related to the martyrs. Xiong Ye also said. He had been deeply stimulated. And was tired of this world. And did not want to live in this world anymore. Buping was very surprised to hear this. And thought to himself. How could someone like him become so passive? Wasn't that strange? At the time, I did not want to ask in detail. And planned to slowly ask him to explain. Unexpectedly, Xiong Ye suddenly disappeared from Huanghuagang. And his whereabouts were unknown.

In an instant, two years had passed. In these two years. Chen Buping sometimes thought of Xiong Ye. Although we were not close friends. I still felt very concerned. And longed to see him. But he had been gone for two years. And I had not heard any news. He had said that he was tired of the world. Perhaps he was no longer in this world. Until last New Year's Day. Buping accidentally walked out of the house. And suddenly saw several people on the hill in the distance. When I went closer. One of them seemed to be Xiong Ye. Who had just finished worshiping at the tomb of the seventy-two martyrs. There was also a wreath placed on the tomb. And offerings of incense, flowers, wine, and food. This was also strange. Usually, no one cared about this tomb. How could someone suddenly come to worship on New Year's Day? The person who looked like Xiong Ye. Although his clothes were very plain. His face was very plump. Completely unlike the haggard person from two years ago. So I was skeptical. Who knew that Xiong Ye still recognized Buping. And quickly came over to shake hands and exchange greetings. Buping was overjoyed and said. "Why did you leave for two years. Without telling me? You must be successful now." When Xiong Ye heard the word successful. He suddenly looked sad and said. "What success are you talking about to me." After a pause, he said. "I originally wanted to have a good talk at your house. But my army is going to depart tomorrow. And I am very busy. So I cannot delay." Buping said. "Oh, you are indeed successful. May I ask what military position you hold now." Xiong Ye said. "I am just participating in the military staff. But my ambition is not to become an official. So I do not want to leave any traces of anything. I can only simply tell you. I want to carry out my father's ambition. My mother also often taught me. Not to be obsessed with forms and power. To be able to live like my father for the rest of my life. Would be considered as carrying on the family tradition. In the past, I thought that the trend was. It was not as good as before the birth of the Republic of China. When my father still had the opportunity to become a martyr. So I felt discouraged. Unexpectedly, there is still today. Which can make me and my mother feel a little comforted. And my father in the ground will also be happy. Today is New Year's Day. So I came to my father's tomb to report. However, although I am a little comforted. There are still many things that are not as I want. If I am not happy. My father in the ground will naturally not be happy. If I continue to work hard this year. And can do everything as I wish. Then next New Year's Day. I will still come here to silently report. At that time, we will have a pleasant conversation." These words. Buping seemed to understand. But also seemed not to understand. When I wanted to ask again. Xiong Ye had already left with the people who came with him.

Buping felt a sense of loss. After returning home. I missed Xiong Ye even more. Time passed quickly. And another year had passed. Buping thought to himself "This year. There has been much more progress than last year. Xiong Ye will always come to his father's tomb on New Year's Day. I must wait for him."

Newly Appointed Director of Zhejiang Education Department Takes Office Formally 125

The newly appointed Director of the Zhejiang Education Department, Zhang Daofan, arrived in the province the day before yesterday, as previously reported in this newspaper. On the 29th morning, Mr. Zhang sent a letter from the West Lake Hotel to the Education Department's secretariat, informing them that he would arrive at the department at 1:00 PM to assume his duties. He instructed them to inform all sections so he could meet and speak with all staff at that time. At 12:30 PM, accompanied by two staff members, he walked to the department. Secretary Lin Duan assisted him in inspecting the various offices. At 2:00 PM, he convened all staff in the auditorium for an address, stating that the educational administration of the province, under the previous Director's ambition and progress, had achieved remarkable results, which had been commended by the Ministry of Education. Since there were established rules and procedures to follow, he would continue to adhere to them and work diligently. Any necessary improvements would be carefully planned and implemented to avoid being out of touch with the times. Director Zhang stated that he had always been determined to fulfill his duties, aiming for high goals, but the path to success lies in starting from the near and ascending from the low, and he did not want to engage in excessive discussions, lest he fall into empty talk without substance. According to past practice, whenever a new official takes office, the old staff would usually submit their resignations. If they truly believe they have fulfilled their duties, there is no need to follow this custom. After the address, he met with the various secretaries and section chiefs, inquiring in detail about various matters in the department's office. He also appointed Zhang Yiyang as the receiving officer to take over the general affairs and accounting matters.

Furthermore, it is reported that the new Education Director, Zhang Daofan, and the Construction Director, Shi Ying, held an inauguration ceremony at 10:00 AM on the 30th morning in the provincial government auditorium. Zhang Nanxian, sent by the central government, served as the oath-taking commissioner. After the ceremony was performed according to protocol, they were separately conferred with seals and took the oath. After the oath-taking commissioner delivered an address, Mr. Zhang responded by stating that he was not yet fully aware of the educational administration and financial situation in the province, and therefore dared not lightly propose plans. However, he emphasized that no matter what kind of undertaking, success requires collective effort, and he hoped that everyone would provide guidance at any time, and he would strive to realize it within the realm of possibility.

Luo Jialun Cables Central Political School Education Director 126

|Yesterday, telegram to Chairman Jiang|

Willing to assist in the capacity of school committee member

Following the Central Standing Committee's decision on December 25th to appoint Luo Jialun as the Director of Academic Affairs and Acting Director of Education at the Central Political School, Mr. Luo immediately telegraphed Chairman Jiang, the school's president, requesting that the central government rescind the order. The original telegram stated, "Mr. Yu Jingtang has been effectively managing academic affairs, and his resignation should not be accepted. Mr. Ding Dingcheng is an elder statesman and a highly respected senior member of the party and the country, and I dare not take over the position of Acting Director of Education. Please forward this request to the central government to rescind the order. I, Luo, am willing to assist in all matters in the capacity of a school committee member." However, it is reported that after Mr. Luo sent the telegram, the central government still telegraphed him urging him to go to Nanjing. Mr. Luo plans to travel to Nanjing within the next few days to present everything in person.

Local News

Sixth Anniversary of the National Language Movement 127

The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association launched the National Mandarin Movement on January 1, 1926. Eighty-six locations across the country, as well as in Nanyang and Japan, simultaneously held Mandarin Movement meetings and resolved to hold a National Mandarin Movement Commemoration Meeting every year on January 1 to awaken the public and promote Mandarin education. January 1st this year marks the sixth anniversary of the National Mandarin Movement. The association held separate commemoration meetings in the capital, Shanghai. The commemoration ceremony was held this morning, and a luncheon was held in the afternoon. A celebration meeting will be held on the 10th. It is also reported that Anqing, Nanchang, Hankou, Wuchang, Changsha, Xiamen, Shantou, Guangzhou, Hangzhou, Tianjin, Singapore, Nagasaki, Osaka, and other places will also hold commemoration meetings locally, organized by fellow members of the association.

Jinan Alumni Association New Year's Gathering 128

Also a farewell to the entire Philippine expedition team

The Jinan University Alumni Association is scheduled to hold a New Year's get-together on the second day of the lunar new year at noon on the eighth floor of the Hua An Company. At the same time, the entire Philippine expedition team will be bid farewell, and a "Ever-Victorious Army" banner will be presented. New graduates from this year will also be welcomed into the association, and President Zheng and Director Ke Chengmao will be invited. This gathering will replace the winter conference, so there will be discussions on fundraising to build the association's headquarters.

Today, Liangjiang to Hold 129

Tenth Anniversary and New Building Inauguration Ceremony

The Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School on Daji Road was founded in 1921 and has been through ten years. At that time, the school rented premises on Dengtu Road in Hongkou, with only a few humble buildings and only seventeen students. Principal Lu Lihua, recalling the past, is overcome with emotion at the changes. It has been decided to hold the tenth anniversary celebration on New Year's Day, 1932. The new steel-reinforced concrete school building, with two four-story buildings, was completed in the autumn of 1930. Due to the usual busy schedule of school affairs, there was little spare time. Now, taking advantage of the New Year holidays, the new school building inauguration ceremony will also be held. Five thousand invitations were sent out in advance, inviting people from all walks of life to attend and provide guidance. Fearing that guests would be busy with New Year's celebrations, the school will also be open for three consecutive days for those who cannot attend to visit. The ceremony will be held at 10:00 AM today. It is reported that Mr. Ma Xiangbo, a 92-year-old director of the school, will preside over the ceremony. The school's own military band will play music. The details of the ceremony are as follows: 1) All attendees take their seats; 2) Music plays; 3) Sing the Party song; 4) All attendees pay their respects to the Party, the National Flag, and the portrait of the Founding Father; 5) The Chairman respectfully reads the Founding Father's will; 6) Students sing the school song; 7) The Chairman delivers the opening remarks; 8) The Party representative delivers remarks; 9) The representative of the administrative organs delivers remarks; 10) The school board member delivers remarks; 11) The faculty member delivers remarks; 12) Guests deliver remarks; 13) The Chairman delivers a response; 14) Music plays; 15) The ceremony concludes; 16) Photograph; 17) Guided tour; 18) Refreshments. The school originally planned to publish a commemorative album to distribute to all sectors, but the printing house could not finish in time, so a commemorative badge will be given instead. Many inscriptions and poems have been received, including those from the heads of various academies, ministers of various ministries, provincial chairmen, provincial directors, and Mayor Zhang and Commander Xiong of the city, as well as directors of various bureaus, a dazzling array of beautiful items. It is reported that they will all be displayed today. The school's ninth graduation ceremony will also be held today.

Guangzhao Public School Art Exhibition 130

Calligraphy artwork won a gold medal at the Belgian Exposition

The Guangzhao Public School on North Sichuan Road, near Yokohama Bridge, is holding an exhibition of calligraphy, painting, and handicrafts for three days, starting today, to promote art education. Amateur photography works by teachers, students, and alumni will also be exhibited. All are welcome to visit, and no admission tickets are required. The school places particular emphasis on calligraphy. This year, the school sent its calligraphy artwork to participate in the Belgian Centennial Independence Exposition, where it won a gold medal. Over the years, the school has also received positive comments from calligraphers Zheng Xiaoxu, Wu Changshuo, and Pan Lanshi.

Sports

Farewell 132

Jinan Team Sets Off Southward

|Starting on the 6th of this month, they will depart for the Philippines|

Amidst the festive sounds of the New Year and the celebration of peace and prosperity, the most exhilarating news is that the Jinan University football and basketball teams will depart south on January 6th to participate in the International Charity Grand Competition at the invitation of the Philippine Sports Association. Such a grand event is unprecedented in the nation, marking a new era in Chinese university sports. This journey is truly akin to being a "sports ambassador," and therefore, as they prepare to depart, we cannot help but offer our warmest wishes and hope that Jinan University will lead the way, and we eagerly await good news.

Principal Zheng's Farewell Speech 133

Vast China, glorious Han people, possessing 400 million people, with a history of over 4,000 years, occupying 30 million square miles of land, but facing increasing foreign troubles and national humiliation. Shouldn't we, upon hearing the story of the ancients rising to dance at the crowing of the rooster and striking the oars in the middle of the river, resolutely rise up and strive forward? I remember that whenever our Founding Father thought of this, he would dance and shout to awaken the people. The legacy he left in people's hearts was to uplift the nation and eliminate all unequal treaties. To achieve this goal, it is essential to promote national physical education and revitalize the national spirit. Jinan University, the highest institution of learning for overseas Chinese, is also the only overseas Chinese education institution in the country that the Founding Father paid the most attention to. The school usually places great emphasis on student physical education. In recent years, the school's sports performance has been outstanding among universities in the country, but we always feel that we must continue to work hard and live up to the Founding Father's legacy. This spring, the school's football and basketball teams were invited by the Philippine government to participate in the National Sports Games at the Carnival. Before their departure, a special publication will be released. I believe that this event is extremely important for international friendship, and this friendship competition with a Chinese university team marks the first page in the history of Chinese sports. Moreover, our athletes are all children of overseas Chinese. The overseas Chinese elders and youth in the Philippines want our school teams to participate in the competition to promote the martial spirit of our country, which is the focus of public attention and the aspiration of all hearts. I believe that our athletes are ready to depart, flying the banner of invincibility and living up to the enthusiasm of our overseas compatriots. This is a great event. However, I deeply hope that our students will not only display the skills and indomitable spirit of our school's teams in the Philippines but also demonstrate the thousands of years of benevolence and chivalry of our nation. That is what I deeply hope for. As for the people of that country and the overseas Chinese in the Philippines, it is hoped that they will provide assistance to our school's team in this trip, which is of great importance to international honor. (Zheng Hongnian)
